British Historian Speaks on the Pacific Problem: Chinese Are Gradually Losing Faith in Western Justice; Future Development of Far East Situation Will Not Exceed Two Paths 39

(London) Moore, a prominent British historian and chairman of the National Liberal Federation, spoke in London today on the Pacific problem, stating: "The weakness and poverty of China have an unparalleled significance for the world. The situation in the Far East progressed steadily until 1929. After 1929, China's finances were in disarray, and the situation deteriorated further and further until the rulers of Japan abandoned their policy of participating in the collective system. The League of Nations and the countries of the world could neither force Japan to abide by its accepted obligations nor protect China to allow it to develop gradually. Today, the unfortunate Chinese cannot help but lose their faith in Western justice and will. Although the Chinese people hate their eastern neighbor, the blood relationship between China and Japan is closer than that with the West, which is still felt by the Chinese people. From now on, the situation in the Far East will not exceed two paths. One is that the Chinese people will follow the path of Western progress, engage in construction, and become self-reliant. The other is that they will join hands with Japan and tell the world, 'Given the current situation, we have no choice but to join the Japanese side to create a strong Eastern power to dominate the world.' If China takes this last step, the rest of the world will not be able to sleep soundly. Although I personally hope that China will still take its own path, whether this hope can be realized is indeed a major question for the future world." (Havas, 3rd)

Arctic Flight to America Forced to Turn Back Mid-Flight Due to Oil Leak, Safely Lands at Leningrad Airport: Soviet Aviator Suffers First Setback 41

(Moscow) The highly anticipated Moscow-San Francisco flight via the North Pole commenced yesterday, but encountered its first setback when the crew discovered a lubricating oil leak, causing excessive oil consumption. Unable to ascertain or rectify this unexpected problem, they immediately telegraphed the Northern Sea Route Administration, requesting permission to return to an airfield in the Leningrad region. Upon receiving approval, the aircraft turned back from the southern Barents Sea, heading towards the Kola Peninsula, the White Sea, and Petrozavodsk, returning to Leningrad. Twenty-two and a half hours after departing Moscow, the Northern Sea Route Administration received a second report stating that the aircraft had safely landed at an airfield south of Leningrad. A new committee has been formed to investigate the various causes of the lubricating oil malfunction during the flight. (4th TASS Dispatch)

(Moscow) The ambitious attempt by Soviet aviator Levanevsky to fly from Russia to San Francisco via the North Pole has failed, at least temporarily. However, determined to showcase the skills of Soviet aircraft and personnel to the world, Soviet authorities will not completely abandon this endeavor. Nevertheless, this setback has caused great disappointment throughout Russia. This morning at 4:00 AM (British Summer Time), Mr. Levanevsky took off with two assistants. According to a radio report sent at 1:20 PM the same day, they had flown over the White Sea and Vony, on the northern coast of the Barents Sea. However, after Mr. Levanevsky departed from the Kola Peninsula, he reported that the gasoline injector was malfunctioning, resulting in significant fuel consumption. Although the aircraft was safely flying over the Arctic Ocean, Mr. Levanevsky telegraphed a request to return to Russia. Upon receiving approval, he immediately turned back and safely arrived at the airfield south of Leningrad at 10:30 PM tonight. Mr. Levanevsky decided to abandon his 6,000-mile flight after traveling 1,000 miles of the planned route, which was to pass through the North Pole, Alaska, Fort Simpson in Canada, Vancouver, and then along the coast to California. The aircraft he was piloting was a specially designed monoplane with retractable landing gear and a 500-horsepower engine, manufactured in the Soviet Union. This morning's flight averaged over 80 miles per hour. (2nd Reuters Dispatch)

(Moscow) The Soviet Union is paying extraordinary attention to and takes great pride in the flight between Moscow and San Francisco undertaken by Soviet hero Levanevsky and his valiant comrades. Today, all newspapers carried this news, along with photographs and texts from Mr. Levanevsky himself, as well as Batoukov, Levchenko, the aircraft designer, a renowned journalist, a professor, and Arctic Ocean aviators. They all stated that the journey was extremely difficult, but the aircraft and personnel used were excellent and the preparations were thorough. Before departure, Mr. Levanevsky, Levchenko, and Batoukov telegraphed the entire nation, saying, "We embark with a heart full of the victory of our nation. Our perfect aircraft embodies the strength of our country. The Soviet people form a happy family, and we are fortunate to be members of this family." They also thanked Stalin for his kindness and concern, and Defense Commissar Voroshilov and Heavy Industries Commissar Ordzhonikidze for their invaluable assistance. They concluded by saying that they wished to quickly return to their homeland and joyfully reunite with their comrades. (3rd Havas Dispatch)

US Silver Legislation: Will Likely Be Shelved in This Congressional Session, Silver Advocates Stage Another Fight 48

(Washington) Today, Senator Thomas, a leader of the silver advocates in the Senate, told the Associated Press that if Congress fails to pass legislation regarding silver during this session, there may never be hope for passage again, at least not during President Roosevelt's current term. Mr. Thomas said that he has convened leaders of the silver advocates in both houses for a meeting on August 6, at which time they will consider what to do if the government fails to achieve the two major goals of the silver purchase law. The so-called two major goals are that the Treasury continue to purchase silver until the price of silver reaches $1.29 per ounce, or the silver reserves in the Treasury reach a ratio of three parts gold to one part silver. Mr. Thomas added that the next congressional session will be very short and will not have time to address the silver issue, so he may join forces with the veterans' bonus advocates to stage a final fight. (3rd Kuomintang News Dispatch)

Shao Yuanchong Arrived in Nanjing Yesterday by Plane 52

(Nanjing) Shao Yuanchong completed his inspection of the Northwest, and returned south via the Pinghan Railway from Datong and Taiyuan. He returned to Nanjing by Eurasia plane at 2:00 PM on the 4th, arriving at 6:00 PM. According to the Central News Agency reporter's inquiries about the inspection process, the trip lasted more than four months, covering more than 10,000 li, passing through the provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, Ningxia, Suiyuan, and Shanxi, as far west as Dunhuang. He conducted detailed inspections of the economic construction and people's livelihood in various places, and the results were very clear. The Northwest is rich in resources, no less than the Jiangnan region. Unfortunately, due to backward transportation and culture, there is no way to develop it. Fortunately, local officials in recent years have been working hard to develop it, so prosperity is by no means difficult. However, the country is poor, and the central government should plan a whole concrete method so that priorities can be arranged in order. The most important thing is transportation and water conservancy, which cannot be delayed. The Northwest produces very rich products, and the land is not all barren and bitter. If construction is good and transportation is convenient, there is no need to worry about prosperity. However, the current poverty of the people is beyond our imagination. Taking schools as an example, the hardship has reached the extreme, but the spirit is no less than that of schools in Jiangnan. The inspection results are very detailed, and may be written out for the study of the people of the country, or suggestions may be made to the central government for reference. After returning to Nanjing today, he will take a rest and will not go elsewhere. (4th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Eastern Ping Whole Embankment of the Grand Canal Collapses. Xiaoqing River Also Breaches for a Thousand Zhang. Flood Victims in Eastern Ping Reach 200,000 91

Jinan Communication: The floodwaters from the Yellow River breach converged in Jining. The waters of the lakes and rivers all surged fiercely. As the southward discharge was obstructed, the west bank of Jining Nanyang Lake, the east bank of the Grand Canal, and the north bank of Zhao Wang River all collapsed. The water flowed northward from Jining along the Grand Canal. Wenshang, Dongping, and other counties again reported emergencies. There are many rivers in these counties, all of which converge into the Grand Canal. The Grand Canal, with its high water level, could not discharge the water. Wenshang's Wen River and Dongping's Xiaoqing River breached. Dong'a and Dongping both have a large lake (Dongping Lake). The Yellow River water from the Grand Canal flowed into the lake, but the lake could not contain it. It flooded southwards. The northeast of the Dongping Canal also completely overflowed. Thus, Dongping was surrounded by water on three sides. Not only was the entire county in danger of being submerged, but Dongping and Wenshang were also about to be completely engulfed in the disaster area. Today (the 2nd), according to a telephone message from Dongping, the Yellow River water from Dongping Lake reached the San Guan Temple south of the city, the closest point to the city. A protective embankment was built around the city (a little distance from the city), and water had already started seeping in. County Magistrate Sun Yonghan is currently supervising the construction of embankments at Jinjiakou, southwest of the city, to block the Yellow River water. All government agencies in the city have completely stopped working to assist in the emergency efforts to protect the embankment outside the city. People are in a state of panic. The water from Dongping Lake on the north side reached Wang Gudizhen in Ershilibao, the boundary between Dongping and Donghe, and also flowed southwards. The Xiaoqing River south of the city breached for about a thousand zhang due to the Grand Canal's backflow. It flooded Wenshang to the south. Wenshang, Dongping, and Dong'a have been completely engulfed in the disaster area.

Dongping Communication: The water from the Yellow River breach in Juancheng, western Shandong, flowed northeast towards Dongping with unstoppable force. The west, north, and south sides of Dongping city are now a vast expanse of water. Many villages have been submerged, with only the rooftops visible. Over 7,000 qing of farmland and over 600 villages have been flooded. Over 300,000 people have been affected. The loss of houses and crops is over 30 million. The exact number of deaths of humans and livestock is still unknown. The immense scale of the flood is unprecedented. The county's party and government officials and people from all walks of life are rescuing people, retrieving livestock, providing porridge, and distributing food. However, as the Yellow River water rises daily, the disaster area expands further. The county has exhausted its financial and physical resources and desperately hopes for relief and assistance from all sides.

Gucheng Suffers Another Flood Disaster, Thousands Drown in Cities and Villages. Landslide Causes Collapse of City Walls and Buildings. Impossible to Distinguish Land From Water. Dragon Eggs with Embryonic Form Found and Sent to Hankou for Display. 92

Hankou Communication: Gucheng, located upstream on the Yao River, faces Laokou, Guanghua, across the river. At the beginning of last month, the river rose violently, causing an unprecedented disaster. The county was also submerged in a large flood. Although the water receded relatively quickly, the current was too swift, and the losses suffered were no less than those in Xiangfan, Tianmen, and Hanchuan. Before long, another disaster struck. On the 1st of this month, the water level of the South River in the county rose again, with the water head over ten zhang high. The land on both banks that had been receding was submerged again. The replanted autumn crops were completely buried in sand. Countless surviving homes collapsed. On the 2nd, the water rose further, directly threatening the city walls. County Magistrate Chen and the 82nd Division of the stationed army had blocked the city gates and hired many boats to prepare for rescue. The seriousness of the situation can be imagined. Cheng Zerun, the Administrative Inspector of the Eighth District and County Magistrate of Xiangyang, reported to Provincial Chairman Zhang Qun via telegram on the 3rd based on a telegram from the Gucheng County government.

The first major disaster in the county could not be learned due to the flooding of the highways, the destruction of the telegraph lines, and the interruption of transportation. According to a detailed investigation, every time it rained in the county, which is at the intersection of mountains and rivers, the ditches and valleys were filled, and low-lying areas were submerged. However, the water would recede when it cleared up. On July 3rd, there was a heavy downpour that lasted all day and night. Residents regarded it as a normal occurrence and did not prepare. The heavy rain continued non-stop. On the evening of the 5th, the North and South Rivers suddenly rose, and the Xiang River broke its banks, flooding the entire county and reaching the city walls. On the evening of the 6th, the water rose another ten zhang. A landslide on the South River caused the collapse of dozens of zhang of city walls on the east, west, and south sides of the county seat. The city became a vast expanse of water. The residents suddenly encountered a major disaster and had no way to escape. Most of the old, weak, women, and children were swept away by the flood. The strong either climbed onto the rooftops or squeezed into the treetops to wait for dawn. The soil in the area is very loose, and the houses are not very sturdy, collapsing as soon as they were exposed to water. The sound of collapsing houses continued all night. Those who took refuge on the roofs could not escape being drowned or buried under the collapsed houses. At that time, the county government building was submerged, and the county magistrate and staff were trapped in the water. There were no boats to be found inside or outside the city. Rong Jingfang, commander of the 82nd Division, immediately sent a company of soldiers, braving the danger, to hire dozens of civilian boats and set off into the Xiang River to rescue the flood victims outside the city. Rong personally supervised the rescue of flood victims outside the city, and sent boats to the Shaanxi Guild Hall, rescued all the staff of the Special Party Department of the division, and worked together to help the refugees. Over two days, they rescued 5,000 flood victims and set up shelters. On the evening of the 8th, people from all walks of life organized a flood relief committee and elected Shen Liang, standing committee member of the Special Party Department of the 82nd Division, as the chairman of the committee. Five groups were set up: general affairs, medical rescue, food distribution, investigation, and discipline. Work began that night. On the morning of the 9th, boats were sent to the surrounding villages to rescue and shelter a total of 20,000 people. The military provided funds to set up factories and distribute porridge. It is said that the funds were entirely donated by Commander Rong. Because of the distance from the province and the disruption of communications, there was no time to ask for relief. The local area was devastated and had no money to raise. On the 9th, the water stabilized, and after the 10th, it gradually receded. A post-disaster investigation revealed that the greatest losses occurred in the urban area and the first, second, and third districts, followed by the fifth district, and then the fourth and sixth districts. Because the water came too violently, many people died. In addition to those swept away by the water, over 10,000 floating corpses were found within the area. Over 20,000 livestock died. The Special Party Department of the 82nd Division, the military hospital, the political training office, and the security team organized a burial team to retrieve and bury over 3,000 human corpses. The stench was overwhelming due to the scorching sun, and all those who participated in the work became ill. The exact number of houses that collapsed is still unknown. The towns and villages in the first, second, and third districts have been razed to the ground. It is impossible to distinguish land from water. The area outside the south gate of the county seat is the commercial center, and was the most deeply flooded. No goods were saved. The magnitude of the loss is unprecedented. During the flood, a myth spread among the people that groups of dragons were swimming in the North and South Rivers, with waves rising and falling together, witnessed by many people. However, the fact that the army found two dragon eggs in a collapsed city wall base in front of the nursery garden in the South City when digging holes to drain the water is indeed a fact. One was damaged by the excavator shaking it, but the other was intact. Upon dissection, it had already taken embryonic form, with the head and mouth resembling a dragon. Shen Liang, standing committee member of the Special Party Department of the 82nd Division, placed it in an alcohol bottle and sent it to Hankou for display. A mountain on the South River completely collapsed. The power of the water was insufficient to cause this, so it was likely caused by dragons. (The 3rd)

Guangdong Province Celebrates "August 1st" Commemoration with Resolution of Government and People to Abolish Exorbitant Taxes and Fees 93

Guangzhou Communication: The "August 1st" Commemoration is a unique commemoration in Guangdong Province, and it is also the first commemorative day of this year. The so-called "August 1st" Commemoration is the anniversary of the abolition of exorbitant taxes and fees. Although the province has suffered in recent years due to the decline of the silk industry, the reduction of remittances from overseas Chinese, and the bankruptcy of the rural economy, since the promulgation of the Three-Year Governance Plan, the authorities have been vigorously carrying out industrial construction in order to increase production. At the same time, they have actively reorganized finances and resolutely abolished exorbitant and miscellaneous taxes to ease the burden on the people and gradually restore the rural economy. It is estimated that since the 22nd year of the Republic of China, the province has abolished 21 types of cargo taxes in Nanxiong Meiguan, etc., with an annual revenue of 113,950 yuan; 13 types of miscellaneous taxes in Lechang, etc., with an annual revenue of over 148,000 yuan; one type of brown sugar tax, with an annual revenue of 860,000 yuan; 19 types of Guangzhou West Tax Factory, etc., with an annual revenue of 1,958,000 yuan; banned gambling in 27 counties such as Shunde, with an annual revenue of 1,664,460 yuan; and abolished 42 types of Taipao and Zuo Li taxes, with an annual revenue of over 1,681,200 yuan; and 25 types of business licenses and booth fees of the Foshan Supplementary Lilac Gold Bureau, with an annual revenue of over 68,260 yuan, totaling over 6 million yuan in annual revenue from exorbitant taxes and gambling that have been abolished. The amount cannot be considered small. These exorbitant taxes and gambling were abolished on August 1st of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, and some were scheduled to be abolished on August 1st of the 24th year of the Republic of China. Therefore, the Provincial Council specially proposed to designate August 1st as the Guangdong Abolition of Exorbitant Taxes and Gambling Commemoration Day, both to commemorate the government's resolution to make a fresh start with the people and to celebrate the people's relief from the suffering of exorbitant taxes and gambling. From now on, the people will work together, burying their heads in hard work and striving to build production. This also shows the beginning of Guangdong's new future. The Provincial Council and the Provincial Party Department have jointly organized various groups to prepare for the "August 1st" Commemoration, which is indeed very meaningful.

Ningbo Chamber of Commerce Implements Measures to Relieve Financial Crisis, Restricts Withdrawal of Deposits Temporarily, Requests Loans From Three Banks for Relief 94

Ningbo Communication: Since July 30th, a number of Qian Zhuang (traditional Chinese banks) in Ningbo, including Yiyuan, Xinyuan, Yongyuan, Wuyuan, Taiyuan, Taisheng, Hengmao, Weikang, Xingyuan, and Yikang, have successively closed down. Unexpectedly, yesterday (the 2nd), five major same-trade organizations, including Taihan, Huiyuan, Yufeng, Jingyuan, and Yuyuan, and eight minor organizations, including Baoyuan, Taixun, Baohe, Yuancheng, Chengyuan, Fengda, and Tongtai, were also affected by the withdrawal of deposits and suspended operations. The Yin County government not only issued a notice restricting depositors to withdrawing only 100 yuan in cash per day, but also ordered the Chamber of Commerce to work with the silver and money industries to quickly develop measures to address the situation. The Chamber of Commerce convened an emergency meeting at 4 PM yesterday (the 2nd), attended by over 50 leaders of the financial community, including Yu Zuochen, Ruan Jiaxian, Jin Keqiang, Hong Chensheng, Lu Ruikang, Chen Xiangyu, Zhang Puful, Zhang Xingzhi, Zhu Xuchang, and Yu Runquan. Zhao Cicsheng, the Administrative Inspector of the Fifth District, Chen Baolin, the County Magistrate of Yin County, and Ni Weixiong, the Chief of Construction Section, were also present. The meeting was chaired by Yu Zuochen, and six resolutions were made on the spot to provide relief: (1) No single Qian Zhuang's shortfall should exceed 150,000 yuan. If the shortfall exceeds 150,000 yuan on a given day, the excess amount will be split up by the same-trade organizations and jointly responsible. (2) From today, the amount of deposits that can be withdrawn per household per day shall not exceed 100 yuan. The Yin County government has issued a notice explicitly restricting this, and all Qian Zhuang shall abide by it. (3) If the Qian Zhuang Association Committee believes that a particular Qian Zhuang has too many shortfalls, it may investigate the number of split shortfalls at any time, and if necessary, order it to fill the shortfalls. (4) It is hoped that the local banks will temporarily not accept transfers of deposits. (5) Request the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications to jointly lend 2 million yuan in national currency to provide relief. (6) All closed Qian Zhuang shall resume operations immediately, and payment clearing will be handled as before, and a copy of the receipts and payments shall be sent to the Chamber of Commerce for review and forwarded to the county government for verification. At the same time, all shareholders will do their best to increase capital, and all depositors will temporarily refrain from withdrawing deposits. After the discussion, Commissioner Zhao and Magistrate Chen gave instructions, and the Chamber of Commerce issued a statement to reassure depositors. The abnormal tension and panic in Ningbo's financial circles in recent days are expected to gradually calm down. As for the large and small Qian Zhuang that announced their liquidation yesterday (the 2nd), the details are as follows: (1) Taihan Qian Zhuang, manager Lin Mengfei, is the current chairman of the Qian Zhuang Association, with a capital of 50,000 yuan and an annual total receipt and payment of approximately 100,000-200,000 yuan. (2) Huiyuan Qian Zhuang, manager Wang Yusheng, with a capital of 55,000 yuan and a total turnover of 1 million yuan. (3) Yuji Qian Zhuang, manager Zhang Zhifang, with a capital of 66,000 yuan and a total turnover of 1 million yuan. (4) Jingyu Qian Zhuang, manager Zhao Shiquan, with a capital of 55,000 yuan and a normal turnover of over 1 million yuan. (5) Yuyuan Qian Zhuang, manager Xu Maotang, with a capital of 66,000 yuan and a total turnover of over 800,000 yuan. The above five organizations are all large same-trade organizations that were implicated and suspended due to the impact of other same-trade organizations. (1) Baoyuan Qian Zhuang is a leading small same-trade organization in Ningbo. The year-end calculation last year showed a significant profit, with a capital of 24,000 yuan and receipts and payments of approximately 500,000 yuan. (2) Taixun Qian Zhuang, with a capital of 22,000 yuan and receipts and payments of approximately 500,000 yuan. (3) Baohe Qian Zhuang, with a capital of 33,000 yuan and receipts and payments of approximately 700,000 yuan. (4) Yuancheng Qian Zhuang, with a capital of 44,000 yuan and receipts and payments of approximately 400,000 yuan. (5) Chengyuan Qian Zhuang, with a capital of 33,000 yuan and receipts and payments of approximately 500,000 yuan. (6) Fengda Qian Zhuang, with a capital of 33,000 yuan and receipts and payments of 380,000 yuan. The above six organizations are small same-trade organizations that were suspended due to being unable to cope with the withdrawal of deposits. In addition, Tongtai Exchange Shop was established solely by Shi Yunsheng, who served as manager, with a capital of 6,000 yuan. It had been open for over 20 years. Due to the tight credit of both large and small same-trade organizations and the rush to withdraw deposits, it was forced to close down. It is reported that the shop had deposits of approximately 40,000 yuan and loans of approximately 100,000 yuan. After offsetting the receipts and payments, there was still a surplus of 20,000 yuan. It is said that after the crisis subsides, they plan to regroup and continue operations. (The 3rd)

Songjiang: Major Gambling Den Cracked Down Upon Outside the West Gate

The He Zan Club at Qianjing Bridge outside the West Gate was raided by the third division of the County Public Security Bureau yesterday. Five gamblers, Mao Zuyi, Xu Baisheng, Cao Xinheng, Zhang Yingxiang, and Liu Jinheng, were arrested on the spot, along with two sets of magpie tiles, one set of Pai Gow tiles, and complete smoking paraphernalia. They were all taken to the County Bureau that night. After a brief interrogation by Director He, Mao Zuyi, considered the most important, was detained for further questioning, while the others were temporarily released on bail. They will be sent to the county for legal proceedings approximately one week from today.

Jiading: Enclosing Ye Pond to Commemorate Martyrs

When the Manchus entered China, the martyrs Hou Tongzeng and Huang Chunyao resisted the foreign race and bravely defended the city. They were eventually outnumbered, and on the day the city fell, Hou drowned himself in Ye Pond to die for his country. His loyalty and righteousness shine brightly in the annals of history. The pond is now located next to the west side of the Education Bureau. Due to its age, it has fallen into private hands, and most of it has been filled in. In order to preserve historical sites, the county government proposed and decided at the political affairs meeting on the 3rd of this month to take the pond under public management and embellish it to promote the martyrs and encourage people.

Implementing a Tax on Banquets to Promote Free Education 95

The county government received an order from the province to promote compulsory education. Fifteen additional classes must be established within this year. In addition to the funds allocated by the province, the local area must raise at least half of the funds itself. Therefore, the method of levying a tax on banquets was proposed and decided at the political affairs meeting on the 3rd. The tax rate is set at 5%, and no tax will be levied on those less than one yuan. The tax will be levied first in the urban and rural areas and in Nanxiang. Once the approval of the provincial authorities is obtained, merchants will be invited to bid to undertake the task.

Nine Robbers Apprehended in Theft Case in Nanguang 96

In the case of the robbery of over 1,200 yuan in cash and gold jewelry from the brothers Guan Jiquan and Guan Qiuquan, farmers of Beiguan Village, Nanguang Township, First District, last month, Guan Jiansheng, a resident of the same village, was identified by the victims as being present at the scene. When investigators went to his home to inquire, his wife claimed that he was not at home, raising strong suspicions. He was detained and confessed that eight other people, including Li Aqiua, were involved. All were detained for questioning.

Suzhou: Female Passenger Jumps Out of Train Window on Shanghai-Nanjing Railway

On the morning of the 4th, the 12th express train from Shanghai on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway was approaching Yangqi outside Zhengyi, east of Suzhou, at 10:43 AM when a fashionable young woman suddenly jumped out of the train window in a second-class carriage to commit suicide. The train stopped immediately, and people in the carriage rescued her. She was taken to Fuxi Hospital at Suzhou Station for treatment. Her injuries were severe, but she was still conscious. The woman identified herself as Wen Ying, 28 years old, from Yunnan, living in Shanghai. Her husband, Peng Chi, is an active-duty military officer. She refused to reveal the reason for her suicide. She carried a leather bag and a rattan basket, containing 90 yuan in banknotes, a gold bracelet, and several slips of paper with correspondence addresses, one was "Yi Ren, Dormitory No. 120, Moore Memorial Church, Shanghai", one was "Sending Dormitory, Shanghai Women's Progressive Association", one was "No. 57 West Amherst Road, French Concession, Shanghai", one was "Quan Shao Tang, c/o Jin Shao Meng, No. 64 Qiao, Longmen, Kunming, Yunnan." However, she suffered a severe head injury, so there may be concerns about the accuracy of the name.

Training All Village Chiefs 97

The Wuxian government is handling the training of village chiefs in the counties and towns. The training of county and town chiefs has been temporarily postponed. However, the training of village chiefs is still underway. Preparations have been completed, and training is scheduled to begin today (the 5th) at the Sanyuanfang Industrial Vocational School. Over 1,000 village chiefs from the entire county reported yesterday (the 4th). The opening ceremony will be held this morning, followed by the start of training, which will last three weeks. Organizing a Stray Dog Shelter 98

The Wuxian Public Security Bureau ordered the start of killing stray dogs from the first day of this month. Over 500 stray dogs were killed in three days, and the killing is still continuing. According to Director Zhang, the killing must continue until all stray dogs are killed. The Religious Philosophy Research Society has initiated the organization of an animal protection association with the aim of saving stray dogs' lives. They held a meeting at their association headquarters on Pingmen Road yesterday (the 4th) and decided to organize a stray dog shelter. The location of the shelter is Niuwang Temple outside the city gate. Preparations are starting immediately, and the Public Security Bureau will be asked to postpone capturing stray dogs.

Giant Bribery Case in Changshu Dismissed 99

The widely publicized giant bribery case in Changshu's Shatou has been under investigation by the prosecutor's office of the Wuxian District Court since it was referred by the High Court. Three months have passed, and the investigation has now concluded. The defendants, Yang Zaitian and Jiang Jizhou, were both given a dismissal.

Wuxi: Press Association Again Requests Revision of the New Publication Law

The local press association, in order to appeal for the revision of the publication law, has dispatched representative Su Xingwu to Suzhou and Changzhou counties to contact and co-sign with their colleagues. He returned to Wuxi yesterday after completing the task. Over 40 colleagues from the Suzhou Mingbao, Wuxian Daily, Zhongshi Township Public Report, Changzhou Wujin Commercial Report, Wujin News, Changshu, and Jiangyin unanimously advocated a full revision of the publication law. Representatives of the newspapers will gather in Wuxi on the 9th and go to Beijing on the 10th to petition. The local press association and its colleagues from the co-signing counties will not only present their case to the Central Propaganda Committee and the Ministry of Interior to request a review of the revision, but also present their case to the Central Political Committee and the Legislative Yuan to revise the Sichuan version of the law, and request appropriate remedies for the crime of defamation under criminal law.

South Bridge Sock Factory Labor Strike 100

The South Bridge Sock Factory in South Bridge Town was founded by Xu Xianchang and has over 100 sock machines and over 100 female workers. The original wages were 18 cents per dozen for #132 socks, 20 cents per dozen for #188 socks, and 21 cents per dozen for #200 socks. Recently, in order to increase work efficiency and production, the factory revised the wages, providing that for #132 socks, the wage would be 15 cents per dozen for more than 30 dozen per month, 16 cents per dozen for more than 40 dozen, and 17 cents per dozen for more than 50 dozen. As each female worker, in accordance with past practice, makes at most 40 dozen per month, this new regulation is called a wage increase in name, but in reality is a wage reduction. The female workers expressed dissatisfaction and repeatedly negotiated, but to no avail, and went on strike yesterday. The situation is currently being mediated.

Escaped Prisoners Re-Imprisoned 101

On the night of the 24th of last month, eight gamblers, including Gu Shaoquan, Huang Genda, Shi Xiaogou, petty thief Wang Yousheng, and drug dealer Bao Kunfu, and Chen Asan suddenly escaped from the detention center of the Sixth Precinct of the Public Security Bureau on Guangyi Road. Afterwards, the head of the precinct dispatched police officers to track them down, but they were not found. The precinct head dispatched police officers to the West Gate and South Gate to arrest them. As a result, four escapees, Chen Asan, Bao Kunfu, Wang Yousheng, and Gu Shaoquan, were apprehended and sent to the General Bureau for questioning yesterday. In addition, a opium bubble offender named Li Rongfu escaped from the county government's detention center on the night of the 2nd. The guards Qian Yingquan and Yang Gensheng were negligent and were detained by the county for questioning. County Magistrate Wang instructed Police Chief Wu to strengthen the supervision of the detainees in the detention center and stop receiving visitors.

Nantong: Relieving the Decline of the Native Cloth Industry

The native cloth industry in Nantong has recently suffered a severe decline in sales. Farmers with weaving machines in the countryside have completely stopped working. Local people believe that as the county is a cotton-producing area and native cloth is the only sideline for farmers in the entire county, the impact is extremely large. Experts are discussing remedies. The native cloth market will open next month. Measures will be taken to eliminate substandard cloth. Li Shengbo and the textile technicians of the Cotton Control Association are designing improved weaving machines and are rushing to build a dyeing factory.

The Fourth District Security Command convened a training course for security team leaders from six counties: Tong, Ru, Hai, Chongming, Qidong, and Jinghai. Over 160 graduates from the third class graduated on the 3rd. Peng Longyao, the Chief of Staff of the District, presented them with credentials and conducted political training. All the graduates performed drills.

Haimen: Zhang Du Takes Over the Chongming Security Team Headquarters

Due to insufficient staffing and financial difficulties of the security teams in Qidong and Chongming, the Nantong District Security Command merged the Jiangsu Province Security 20th Brigade. Li, County Magistrate of Qidong, served as brigade commander, and Zhang Du was appointed deputy brigade commander. Li sent Deputy Brigade Commander Zhang to Chongming to take over the Chongming Security Brigade Headquarters. Deng Bixing, County Magistrate of Chongming, handed over everything. On the 2nd, Zhang went from Chongming to Shanghai and then to Nantong to report the takeover situation to the District Command. It is reported that after the team is merged, the District Command will send personnel to inspect and accept the team.

Letter from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance 102

Regarding the examination of the provisions in Article 14 of the Jiangsu Province Business Tax Regulations, which state, "The Department of Finance may, at any time, dispatch personnel to conduct on-site spot checks based on the survey reports of various bureaus," this department dispatched personnel to Wujiang for a spot check. This was done in accordance with the established regulations to verify whether the reported figures were accurate and whether there were any instances of underreporting or omissions. The account books of the Cheng Fuxing Rice Firm in Shengze were the first to be examined. Handling the matter in accordance with regulations and requesting to view the account books was a normal procedure and not a significant issue. However, Cheng Fuxing relied on the guild as a shield and refused the request. The department commissioner and the bureau, finding that the firm was not complying with the regulations and was deliberately resisting, immediately suspended the work and reported the matter to the department, requesting that the Wujiang County Government be instructed to have the Public Security Bureau obtain the accounts. As the county magistrate also served as the Commissioner of Supervision and Collection, he had the authority, according to regulations, to enforce compliance when merchants refused to cooperate with investigations. However, the Shengze Rice Guild sent a telegram to the province, threatening a complete work stoppage by its members. Before the provincial department could respond, they carried out a forced market strike. Simultaneously, Cheng Fuxing and others led a mob to the Business Tax Bureau, destroying everything. Six officials were seriously injured, with two in critical condition. Documents, vouchers, and all other items were completely destroyed. After achieving their goal of destroying the bureau, the rioters, upon hearing a flute call, led the crowd away. At the same time, the rice firms voluntarily resumed normal business operations. Such organized and planned mob violence disturbing public order is intolerable under the law. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has repeatedly ordered that guilds not control business taxes. Yet, the rice guild dared to arbitrarily exert such control, sending telegrams with threats. Despite regulations requiring account checks, Cheng Fuxing dared to resist and disobey. They used a market strike to protest and the destruction of the bureau to demonstrate. If they are not severely punished according to the law, how can order be maintained? In addition to requesting the provincial government to arrest the principal offenders and severely punish them, this letter is specially sent to your esteemed newspaper with the request that it be published in the "Letters to the Editor" section to clarify the truth and prevent misunderstandings. Sincerely, Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, August 3rd.

Donation of Chiang's Aircraft Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday, Reached Hongqiao Airport at 4 PM, Will Be Inspected and Repaired Before Flying to Sichuan 103

A Central News Agency report states that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, to strengthen Sino-Italian relations, specially gifted Chairman Chiang Kai-shek with the latest Savoia-Marchetti S.72 aircraft from Italy. The aircraft departed from Rome on July 6th, passed through Athens, Baghdad, Calcutta, Annam, and arrived in Hong Kong. Due to unfavorable weather, it was delayed for several days. It departed from Hong Kong at 8:15 AM yesterday and arrived in Shanghai at 4:00 PM. The Central News Agency reporter provides the following details:

Welcoming Delegation

The Italian Consulate in Shanghai received a telegram yesterday morning stating that the aircraft had departed from Hong Kong at 8:15 AM. They immediately notified all relevant parties. Hongqiao Road was bustling with traffic. Police were deployed along the route and inside the airport to provide tight security. Those present to welcome the aircraft included: Tang Shixuan, representing the municipal government; Yang Hu from the Municipal Security Bureau; Li Rongyao from the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; Xu Jinyuan, Chief of Staff of the Songhu Garrison Command; Cai Jingjun, Chief of the Municipal Public Security Bureau; Qin Zongfan, Station Master of Hongqiao Airport; Dai Enqi, General Manager of China National Aviation Corporation; Italian Ambassador Galeazzo Ciano and his wife; Advisor Bonalrelli; Aviation Attaché Tenaglia; Chinese Language Attaché Ross; Consul General Narone; Vice Consul Dirle; the captain of the Italian naval vessel Grigoletti; and over three hundred Italian residents. In addition, a small squad of Italian sailors in Fascist uniforms stood in formation at the airport to pay their respects.

Arrived in Shanghai at 4 PM

According to the original schedule, the aircraft was expected to arrive at 1:00 PM. However, due to inclement weather, the flight was delayed. It finally appeared south of Hongqiao Airport at 3:30 PM. Two aircraft from the airport, piloted by Gao Zhihang and others, performed aerial acrobatics. As the Savoia-Marchetti approached, they guided it in a circle around the city before landing precisely at 4:00 PM.

Flight Crew

There were six people on board, including Colonel Scaroin, the pilot; First Pilot Tondi; Second Pilot Chiapparo; Sulussoliu; Bisol; and Peseotori. Upon disembarking, the military attaché dispatched by the Italian Consulate to Hong Kong introduced Colonel Scaroin to each of the welcoming guests.

Welcome Speeches

The Chinese and Italian flags were displayed high atop the airport office. Welcoming staff led Scaroin to the front of the office, where Hongqiao Station Master Qin Zongfan offered champagne and gave a brief welcoming speech. Both sides cheered "Long Live China and Italy!" They then went inside for refreshments and a brief exchange of greetings before heading to the Italian Consulate. Afterward, they went to the Cathay Hotel for rest.

Scaroin's Remarks

The aircraft departed from Rome on July 6th and made stops at various locations along the way. According to Colonel Scaroin, speaking to a Central News Agency reporter, he left Hong Kong at 8:15 AM this morning (yesterday morning). Due to unfavorable weather along the way, his arrival in Shanghai was slightly delayed. He was feeling fatigued upon landing. He had not yet decided how long he would stay in Shanghai or when he would fly to Chengdu. (Scaroin is a world-renowned aviator who shot down 29 enemy aircraft during the European War.)

Will Soon Fly to Sichuan

The aircraft is a single-wing Savoia-Marchetti, painted cream-colored, with the letters ABMO. It has three engines, each with 650 horsepower, totaling 1,954 horsepower. The wingspan is 100 feet, and the fuselage is 60 feet long. It is quite large and imposing and can accommodate ten to twenty passengers. It is reported that the aircraft will undergo inspection and repair in Shanghai before flying to Sichuan. Municipal authorities in Shanghai will host a banquet in the next few days to welcome the crew.

Japanese "Qinghai" Aircraft Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday, Took Off from Fuzhou at Noon and Arrived at 5 PM, Scheduled to Leave Shanghai for Japan in Two or Three Days 104

A Central News Agency report states that the "Qinghai" aircraft, piloted by Japanese pilot Mr. Ano, departed from London, passed through China, and flew back to Japan. After arriving in Hong Kong, the aircraft took off from Hong Kong to Shanghai the day before yesterday. Unexpectedly, the aircraft parts were damaged on the way, and it was forced to land in Fuzhou. It then took off from Fuzhou to Shanghai yesterday afternoon and arrived here at about 5:00 PM that day, landing at Longhua Airport. It is scheduled to leave Shanghai for Japan in two or three days. The details are as follows:

Welcoming Personnel

Those who went to Longhua Airport yesterday to welcome the crew included: Wang Changchun, representing Mayor Wu; Tan Baoshou, Chief Inspector of the Municipal Public Security Bureau; Liang Fuchu, Chief of the Xinzha Public Security Branch; Military Attaché of the Japanese Embassy in China Honno; Naval Attaché Sato; Secretaries Tanaka and Iwai Izumi; Commander of the Special Naval Landing Force Araki; Commander of the Third Fleet Hyakutake; Miss Mieko, daughter of Consul General Ishii; Sugimoto, Chairman of the Japanese Residents' Association of Shanghai; Hayashi, Chairman of the All-Shanghai Japanese Associations; Tanabe, Secretary-General of the Japanese Chamber of Commerce and Industry; Tanno, representative of the Japanese Association; Sato, representative of the Japanese High School; Konishi Tomiko, Okuda Kazuko, Ido Natsuko, Eguchi Mutsumi, and Tanabe Ayako, representatives of the Japanese Higher Girls' School; and representatives of the Nagasaki Prefecture Association, totaling more than 50 people. They all arrived at the airport in the morning and waited until dusk before dispersing.

Arrival in Shanghai

The Qinghai aircraft took off from Fuzhou at 12:30 PM yesterday afternoon to Shanghai, but Shanghai never received confirmation that the aircraft had left Fujian. Welcoming guests all arrived at Longhua Airport in the morning to wait. At 4:00 PM in the afternoon, they looked up at the sky, but still did not see the shadow of the Qinghai aircraft. It was not until about 4:50 PM that the aircraft was seen coming from the south and circling the field once before landing at Longhua Airport at exactly 5:00 PM. Amidst the applause of Chinese and Japanese people, pilot Ano disembarked, received flowers presented by various Japanese organizations and the flag presented by the Nagasaki Prefecture Association, and then walked into the passenger lounge. Sugimoto, chairman of the Japanese Residents' Association of Shanghai, stood up and delivered a welcoming speech, and then everyone raised their glasses to drink "Hakutsuru" and dispersed. Pilot Ano is a young man in his twenties, full of energy and heroic. He stayed at the Tatsumi-kan Hotel on Youheng Road last night.

Ano's Remarks

According to Pilot Ano, he took off from Fuzhou at 12:30 PM this afternoon (yesterday afternoon). Due to the bad weather, after taking off, he always drove in the clouds, struggled hard for more than four hours before breaking out of the clouds. At that time, he found that the gasoline remaining in the aircraft was only enough to support it for 15 minutes. Fortunately, when he looked down, Shanghai was in sight, so he was able to land safely. He originally planned to return to his country via Qingdao, Dalian, and Korea, but now he has decided to stay in Shanghai for two or three days before returning directly to Japan's Oita Air Base.

Ningbo Compatriot Association, Concerned About Hometown Finance, Will Hold a Meeting to Study Revival Methods, Important Suggestions by Zhang Daoyuan of Ningbo 116

Since Datong Heng, Xinyuan, Yiyuan, Taiyuan, Yongyuan, Wuyuan, and other money houses in Ningbo were agitated by the social and economic turmoil and suspended operations, people were panicked and rushed to withdraw deposits. In a few days, more than 20 companies, including Taisheng, Yuyuan, Jingyuan, Huiyuan, Taihan, Yufeng, Yuanheng, and Yuanchun, either suspended operations or were liquidated. This was indeed an unprecedented financial crisis in Ningbo. The impact has affected various ports such as Shanghai, Hangzhou, and Hankou. Although the Yin County government has restricted the number of withdrawals, and the Ningbo Money House Guild has resolved that all will suspend collection and settlement, they are all stopgap measures. Now it is heard that the Ningbo Shanghai Compatriot Association believes that the financial crisis was caused by the money houses themselves, but the depositors did not understand the situation clearly and followed the trend, rushing to withdraw deposits, which seemed to be the main cause of the crisis. Yesterday, a meeting was held to discuss rescue measures, and a special committee will be organized to handle this matter. At the same time, the association also received suggestions from compatriot Zhang Daoyuan, which will also be discussed. The following is an excerpt from Mr. Zhang's letter: In order to contribute opinions, I would like to ask your association to immediately organize the Ningbo Economic Recovery Committee to promote the Ningbo Economic Group in order to save the country. I believe that Ningbo's economy and culture have benefited my country and the international community in a grand and long-lasting way. In the past, Daoyuan drafted an article "The Status of Ningbo City in the History of International Commerce," which was roughly explained. Based on the textual research of his humble work, it can be seen that the modern mercantilism, our Ningbo people, can be called the ancestors. Therefore, they have always had a superior position in the domestic and foreign markets. However, recently, a financial crisis occurred in Shanghai, and the shock and collapse of our Ningbo help turned to suffer again, panting and struggling. The bad news from our hometown is frequent, and the finance is like a mountain and a sea. The root of our Yong economy has been eroded, and our industry and commerce are also like morning dew. Looking around, there are dangers everywhere, and the livelihood of the whole family is almost extinct. Some say that this is due to the attack of the recessionary turmoil, and the shared momentum is irresistible. However, looking back at those who are evenly matched with our Ningbo gang, their financial strength, according to statistics, has made greater progress than last year. Therefore, the industry and commerce supported by their strength can all struggle to prosper. When we examine why they are uniquely good, it is all due to their tangible and intangible group spirit. In the international arena, this kind of economic group, such as the British group and the American group, has done everything possible to restore its prosperity. Now, our Ningbo, with a shared boat and a historical destiny and the legacy of excellent species, has declared the bankruptcy of the domestic economy. Is it not ashamed to die? If we are not brave enough to know our shame and reverse the tide, then in the future, we will have nothing to rely on to survive, and we will only perish together. Daoyuan has attempted to promote the honor of our Ningbo history and has published his rough plans in the newspapers, and what he said is often just a confession. Now, I do not hesitate to take the liberty of submitting my humble opinions to your association, hoping that you will quickly organize the Ningbo Economic Recovery Committee to urgently rescue the economic life of our Ningbo from the brink of extinction for the vanguard of our national revival. I can't help but pray for it.

Summary of the Disaster in Zhide County, Anhui 119

The Chinese Jisheng Society recently received a letter from Lin Jinwen, a member of the Standing Committee of the Disaster Relief and Revitalization Association of Zhide County, Anhui Province, stating that Zhide is located near the Yangtze River, and is known as a rocky city, with many mountains and few fields, a narrow land and a dense population. In years of abundance, the income is not enough to eat. If there is a partial disaster, panic will be seen immediately. Since the spring of last year, bandits and droughts have been combined. There is no surplus of grain in the family, and there are few hidden possessions in the household. Crying for hunger and cold, and wailing are everywhere. There are countless people who have hanged themselves, fallen into wells, and been poisoned to death. In total, more than 10,000 people have died in more than a year. The remaining people who are struggling and suffering are in this catastrophe. The lives of 120,000 people in our county have no chance of survival. Since the beginning of summer this year, there have been continuous rains and disasters, and floods have broken out. The Yangtze River has flowed back, and if the Li Gongwei dam is mentioned, it is the screen barrier attached to the city. Now it has collapsed, and a vast ocean is the result. Residents near the dam, government buildings, and houses are gone. Corpses are floating around. The paddy rice has been washed away. Innumerable livestock have been drowned. The lucky survivors have become refugees. Due to the water vapor and sun exposure, epidemics are prevalent. Disasters are coming one after another. The extreme misery cannot be described. Please urgently allocate huge funds to rescue the survivors so that the people of Zhide will not be filled with ditches. The previous reports have recorded that floods in Anqing, Anhui Province, have broken through dams, houses have been submerged, and people have died tragically. The disaster in Zhide is even more so. The counties along the Yangtze River are even more miserable. The society hopes that the source of revitalization funds is reliable and can be used to save the disaster victims and fulfill their natural duties.

Butchers Petition the Party Department to Thoroughly Investigate Secretly Added Transportation Fees, Expressing Dissatisfaction with the Slaughter Companies 122

Over 1,000 butchers in the Shanghai International Settlement are in dispute due to their opposition to the four slaughter companies, Su-Xi-Ning-Hai, Ning-Hu, and Ren-Yuan, secretly adding transportation fees. They have repeatedly sent representatives to negotiate and sent letters of inquiry, but have not received a response. It is now known that the butchers have decided to jointly petition the Municipal Party Department to investigate. The original text is as follows: "Petition regarding the Su-Xi and other four slaughter companies taking advantage of their power to oppress and secretly add transportation fees for the industry, requesting a strict and thorough investigation to clarify the truth. We, the butchers, purchase pigs from various pig dealers in Wusong. In addition to the original price, we pay a handling fee of one dime, a pre-slaughter inspection fee of one dime, a tying fee of seven cents, and a transportation fee of two dimes (all advanced by the dealers). In the past, due to not understanding the truth, we had once negotiated with the pig dealers in Wusong. Subsequently, the four slaughter companies, Su-Xi-Ning-Hai, Ning-Hu, and Ren-Yuan, took on the responsibility of mediation. As a result, the handling fee was reduced by three cents, and the rest were acknowledged as advanced payments, and a settlement record was signed, declaring the matter resolved. It is now known that the transportation fee is only one dime and five cents per pig according to the transportation company that undertakes the work. The remaining five cents are secretly subsidized by the transportation company to the four slaughter companies, Su-Xi, Ning-Hai, Ning-Hu, and Ren-Yuan, as special expenses. The reason for this is that the slaughter companies take advantage of their power to oppress. When pigs are transported from the pig dealers to the slaughter companies for slaughter, the slaughter companies send staff to inspect them. If there are any shortages or deaths, the transportation company is required to compensate in full. The transportation company cannot bear the pain, so they secretly subsidize the four companies with five cents. According to the transportation company's subsidy, it is ultimately borne by us, the butchers. These four slaughter companies use such means to profit from it. Now that we, the butchers, know the inside story, we can transport the pigs ourselves. However, if we transport the pigs ourselves, the slaughter companies claim that they will refuse to slaughter the pigs. We, the butchers, originally slaughtered at the slaughter companies run by foreigners, and the prices were even cheaper. However, driven by patriotic sentiments, we do not want the rights to flow overseas. In addition, the current slaughter companies are produced by the meat industry association, and the association is also produced by us, the butchers. Now, these four slaughter companies are oppressing the industry in this way, illegally collecting fees, and regarding the association as their own private property, which is extremely illegal. We have repeatedly sent representatives to negotiate and sent letters of inquiry, but they have ignored us. We have no choice but to jointly petition your committee to promptly and thoroughly investigate the illegal fees charged by the four slaughter companies to clarify the truth and meet public expectations. In presenting this, we are extremely eager to await orders. We respectfully present this to the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special City Party Department. Sincerely, over 500 Shanghai butchers, including Lu Gaojian."

Catholic Members Go to Songjiang for Medical Treatment, Tragic Accident on the Way Back, Two Sons and One Grandson of Lu Bohong Seriously Injured, Shi Zongkai Suffered Fatal Injuries and Died on the Spot 123

The Ruose Hospital at the Matou Bridge in Songjiang has a tradition of having members of the Shanghai Chinese Catholic Action Association go there every summer to provide medical treatment and medicine to the poor and sick in the countryside. Yesterday was Sunday, and seven members of the association, Lu Zengzuo, Lu Zengli (son of Lu Bohong), Lu Qinren (grandson of Lu Bohong), Shi Zongkai, Zhou Sanbao, Tan Zhifang, etc., went there with the necessary medicines. They traveled by the Lu family's own car, license number 6500, driven by Lu Zengzuo himself, along the Songhu Highway. After finishing the treatment at about 2:00 PM, they returned to Shanghai in the original car. Unexpectedly, when the car passed Beiqiao and was approaching Zhuanqiao, the two rear wheels of the car suddenly burst at the same time, causing the car to become unmanageable for a while. In addition, the surface of the coal cinder road was uneven, causing the car to sway from side to side. Lu Zengzuo was momentarily careless, and the front of the car crashed into a wooden telephone pole on the side of the road. Lu urgently tried to steer away, but unexpectedly there was a riverbank next to the road. Due to the excessive steering, the car broke the telephone pole, overturned into the riverbank, and plunged into a paddy field with the bottom of the car facing the sky. Everyone in the car was seriously injured and unable to move. Fortunately, a villager caught sight of them and rushed forward to pull the injured out of the car and reported to the Zhuanqiao Township Office, which used the telephone to notify the Lu residence in Shijialong. The Lu residence immediately sent a car to the scene of the accident to transport the injured back. After hearing the news, the reporter went to inquire. It was learned that only the driver, Liu, was not injured. Shi Zongkai was the most seriously injured and had already died. Lu Zengzuo was injured in the waist, Lu Qinren's leg bone was broken, Zhou Sanbao was seriously injured in the head, Lu Zengli had minor head injuries, and Tan Zhifang had minor injuries. All were sent to the Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment to deal with the aftermath of the deceased.

Unable to Bear the Pain of Debt Collection, Zhao Baoquan Commits Suicide, Takes Poison and Goes to the Debtor's Home to Wait for Death, Dies Before Being Rescued at the Hospital 125

Zhao Baoquan, a 47-year-old resident of Nantao Lane, No. 24 Lujiabang, Nanshi, made a living by emptying chamber pots. Because he owed Gong Zhang, a 59-year-old woman residing at No. 47 of the same lane, over 90 yuan in association fees, Gong had repeatedly urged Zhao to pay, but without success. There had been conflicts, which were dispersed by others. The night before, Gong Zhang again asked Zhao Baoquan to pay, but Zhao said that life was becoming more and more difficult, and where would he get extra money to repay the old debt? Moreover, Gong Zhang's residence was nearby, and they saw each other several times a day, and she would urge him to pay whenever they met, making him unbearable. Therefore, Zhao Baoquan suddenly had the idea of committing suicide. So, the night before, he bought six dimes worth of opium and broke into Gong Zhang's house to squat, waiting to die. Gong Zhang initially did not know that he had taken poison. It was not until the poison took effect that Zhao Baoquan's face turned pale and his mind became unclear. Gong Zhang was shocked when she saw this and immediately reported to the police, trying to find a way to rescue him, but it was too late. He died shortly after. The police detained Gong Zhang and took her to the Wenmiao Road Police Station. Yesterday morning, the 27th Xiu Di Bao, Tao Rong, was ordered to report to the local court to request an inquest. Subsequently, Prosecutor Ouyang Shu and Coroner Guan Zhiming were appointed to the scene. It was verified that the deceased, Zhao Baoquan, had died from poisoning. It was ruled that the body be coffined by the deceased's daughter, Mao Zhao. The police station will hand over Gong Zhang to the case after interrogation for investigation.

Ten-Year-Old Murder Case, Suspects Arrested as Accomplices, Zhu Xiaobu Avenges His Brother 127

Zhu He, from Sheng County, Zhejiang, used to run a redwood workshop in Lujiabang, Nanshi. In May of the 14th year of the Republic of China, Wang, the wife of Zhu Sanjin, a clan brother of Zhu He, was beautiful and quite promiscuous. She became acquainted with Xu Sanquan, a worker in the redwood workshop. Unexpectedly, the affair was discovered by Zhu Sanjin, who was consumed by jealousy. He spoke to Zhu He about his wife's adultery, wanting to find an opportunity to catch them and not remain silent. Zhu He advised him to be tolerant for the sake of family honor and repeatedly advised him. He also warned Wang to repent and start anew. Unexpectedly, Wang's wild nature was difficult to tame, and she did not listen to good advice. Soon after, she and her lover, Xu Sanquan, fled together. After Wang fled, Zhu Sanjin resented Zhu He for not stopping them, otherwise he would have brought the adulterer and adulteress to justice earlier. So, he gathered people to negotiate with Zhu He. On the evening of the 27th of that month, at around 10:00 PM, Zhu Sanjin and others gathered at Zhu He's doorstep, called Zhu He outside, and without asking why, hacked at him with axes. Zhu He was outnumbered and was immediately hacked to death. The murderers, seeing that their goal had been achieved, fled in a panic. Afterwards, the local Bao reported to the local court prosecutor, who arrived at the scene and found that the deceased's head had been hacked open and his brains were flowing out. It was confirmed that he had died from the injuries. The body was identified, and three accomplices were arrested, interrogated, and sentenced to 14 years of imprisonment. The sentence was confirmed and they were sent to prison. Unexpectedly, after more than a decade, the old case was brought up again. Zhu Xiaobu, who lives near Beichujiaqiao, is the brother of Zhu He. Recently, he learned that his brother Sanhe was brutally hacked to death and that Hu Yongxing had summoned him out, and that Hu was also an accomplice. He discovered that Hu Yongxing was hiding at No. 33 Tangjia Lane, West of the city. He filed a complaint with the local court prosecutor's office, requesting an investigation. After receiving the complaint, the court secretly ordered police officer Zhang Chunsen to go to No. 33 Tangjia Lane, West Tangjia Lane, to arrest Hu Yongxing, accompanied by the plaintiff Zhu Xiaobu, early yesterday morning, and dispatched a senior police officer from the police station under the jurisdiction of the patrol road. Hu Yongxing was arrested and brought back to the court. Prosecutor Kong Xianglin interrogated him and ordered him to be detained for investigation.

620,000 Red Pills Seized from Rubber Shoes and Pillow Cores in Wooden Boxes, Discovered by Staff at the North Cargo Depot on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, Reported to Be Transported to Xin'an County, Longhai Railway—The Receiving Clerk of the Huitong Transit Company Evades— 131

The North Cargo Depot on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway is located at the intersection of Qiujiang Road and Baoshan Road. At around 10:40 AM yesterday, Mao Fengsui, a cargo clerk at the depot, suddenly felt that two wooden boxes of rubber shoes and pillow cores, reported by the Huitong Transit Company office at No. 799 Qiujiang Road to be transported to Yuda Public and Xinxin Store in Xin'an County, Longhai Road, seemed suspicious when weighing and loading the goods. They did not seem to be the weight of such goods. He asked the reporter of the company to open the boxes, but the reporter claimed that he needed to report to the company and never returned. The depot then, together with Station Master Qi, Section Chief Zhong of the Railway Police Section, and Patrol Officer Hong Wenxin from the North Station Branch, dispatched police officer Wang Xubin to open the two boxes for inspection. It was found that there were two iron boxes, 12 inches long, 7 inches wide, and 5 inches high, each containing 6 packages of red pills. Therefore, the goods in the boxes were completely emptied, and it was discovered that the boxes were two-layered with a height of 5 inches. In the bottom of the boxes, there were 50 packages of red pills, each package containing 10,000 pills, totaling 620,000 pills, weighing 56 kilograms. At that time, the North Station Branch and the two Railway Police Sections immediately reported the discovery of a large number of drugs to their superiors and dispatched senior police officers to the company's office on Qiujiang Road to search. However, the staff at the office had already fled. They issued a notice to the Huitong Police Station and sent detectives to the Huitong General Company at the intersection of Jielu and Kene Hai Road to summon Fang, the accountant and an employee of the company, for questioning. They claimed that the goods were recruited by the company's receiving department, so the director of the receiving department, Pan Lansheng, must be responsible. However, Pan and more than ten employees of the receiving department had already fled. They promised to look for them. Fang and others then signed a guarantee on the spot to go out and investigate. It was not until yesterday that they learned that Pan Lansheng and others were hiding in the Andong Hotel on North Zhejiang Road. They went to the Yongxing Road Police Station to arrest them and take them back to the police section. The office of the company was sealed off by the police, and all the drugs have been sent to the garrison headquarters. The main criminals will be sent for trial after the interrogation is confirmed. As for the responsible personnel of Huitong Company who were summoned, it is said that they are still in Suzhou and have not returned. Therefore, the origin of the drugs and who entrusted them will be revealed soon. It is also known that the company was found by the Road Bureau last month to have committed fraud in the transportation of goods, so the contract for transporting goods signed by the company and the Road Bureau was terminated long ago. Unexpectedly, they are now secretly transporting drugs, which can be said to be disregarding the law.

Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association: Report on the Establishment Process Over the Past Year 133

In Shanghai, considering only the Public Concession, there are nearly 10,000 rickshaws. Directly or indirectly, more than 100,000 people rely on pulling these 10,000 rickshaws for a living. Most of them live extremely hard lives, lack organization and training, and are facing further threats in this global economic downturn. As rickshaw pullers, they are replacing machine power and their livelihoods are under threat. To improve the lives of rickshaw pullers within the Concession, the Public Works Department organized a committee to study improvement plans for the purpose of salvaging the situation. After five months of detailed research, the committee drafted sixteen suggestions for improving the current rickshaw system, and submitted them to the Board of Directors of the Public Works Department. Except for items one, two, and three, which were reserved, the remaining thirteen items were approved by the Board of Directors and a Rickshaw Affairs Committee was established. Massey, Zhu Mao Cheng, and Wang Zhi Ren were invited to serve as committee members to implement the plan. Thus, items such as (1) rickshaw owner registration, (2) rickshaw style improvement, (3) reducing rickshaw rent by 25%, and (4) rickshaw puller registration were actively carried out. At the same time, the Public Works Department also considered the benefits of establishing a rickshaw pullers mutual aid association, and organized a rickshaw pullers mutual aid association management department, which was established on July 13th of last year. The Bureau designated three committee members as custodians. Later, the committee invited social figures Li Denghui, Peng Jin, Xie Andao, Tao Deman, Ying Shugui, Qiu Zitong, Deng Yuzhi, and representatives from the rickshaw businesses Yin Zhiling and Gu Songmao, to form a board of directors, purely for the welfare of rickshaw pullers, based on their own efforts and mutual aid. The board of directors then organized an executive department, inviting Mr. Zhang Dengying to serve as the general manager to carry out all association affairs. As for the association's expenses, each rickshaw was charged seven cents of silver per day, collected by the rickshaw owner on behalf of the association. This burden on the rickshaw pullers was not too difficult, as the Public Works Department reduced the daily rickshaw rent to seventy-eight cents, requiring them to contribute only a few cents per day to the mutual aid association, which was much less than the previous rent of fourteen cents per day. On November 5th of the same year, a temporary general assembly of the rickshaw pullers mutual aid association was established on the upper floor of the Xiaocaichang in Dongjiaxing Road, Hongkou. On the 29th, a western district branch was established in Tailai Lane, McGonigal Road. The association's articles of association and detailed rules for implementation were also amended and approved by the Board of Directors of the Bureau in March of this year. This is a general overview of the establishment of the mutual aid association.

Currently, the outside world seems to have some unclear understanding or incorrect observations regarding the expansion of the association's internal affairs. Therefore, a report on the key points of the current situation inside the association, based on a recent visit, is provided for the attention and reference of all sectors of society.

Current association locations: "General Association" upstairs in the Xiaocaichang, Dongjiaxing Road, Hongkou; "Western District Branch" No. 20, Tailai Lane, McGonigal Road; "Southern District Branch" No. 50, Hengqing Lane, at the southern end of Beiler Road, French Concession; "Nanshi Branch" No. 114, Qinglong Bridge, Xuejia浜; "Zhabei Branch" Nos. 8 and 9, Tonghe Lane, opposite the Shanghai-Taiyuan Motor Vehicle Station, Datong Road.

Regular Activities: (Moral Education) Moral education lectures, various friendship meetings, discussion groups, small group meetings; (Intellectual Education) Children's schools, adult schools, reading rooms, libraries, letter writing services, educational movies, various lectures, literacy campaigns, family education guidance for rickshaw pullers, etc.; (Medical and Health Services) Clinics, home visits, various health initiatives; (Mutual Aid) Providing rice and used clothing, sending seriously ill individuals to hospitals, assisting with funeral expenses, lending small capital, and other services such as planning for the elderly, registering for nearsightedness and providing eyeglasses, providing travel expenses for those returning to their hometowns due to serious illness, providing rice and food for fire and accident victims, and mediating disputes, etc.; (Social Services) Dormitories, economic canteens, rickshaw puller life surveys, bathhouses, 22 roadside tea stands, provision of medicine for heatstroke, various social movements, etc.; (Social and Entertainment Activities) Teahouses, recreation rooms, social gatherings, popular lectures, etc.

Activities Currently in Progress: (Intellectual Education) For rickshaw pullers and their children, in addition to teaching reading and writing skills, handicrafts are also taught as part of the curriculum. Mr. Chen Heqin and others have been invited to serve as education committee members to establish more schools for literacy and handicrafts; (Medical and Health Services) (1) In addition to the existing five clinics, more need to be added; (2) In addition to the existing free bathhouses, several hygienic and inexpensive bathhouses should be established in Zhabei and Nanshi; (3) Expand home visits and medical services; (Relief Services) (1) Rickshaw pullers who have not yet registered are being organized into a "Special Relief Committee for Unregistered Rickshaw Pullers" to find ways to help them make a living, which will soon be realized; (2) Relief will be expanded for all rickshaw pullers who are unable to work due to illness or death; (Social Services) (1) Rickshaw puller group insurance; (2) Savings associations, consumer cooperatives, etc.

Budget for the Next Year: Social insurance, relief, and medical work: 6,815 yuan, accounting for 50%; administrative expenses: 3,390 yuan, accounting for 25%; education and sports activities: 1,153 yuan, accounting for 8%; bathing: 1,415 yuan, accounting for 10%; tea and games: 440 yuan, accounting for 4%; dormitory equipment: 390 yuan, accounting for 3%. According to the association's monthly income, which is approximately 14,885 yuan, and expenditures of 13,603 yuan, there is a surplus, which is said to be used for unexpected needs.

Daily Attendance Figures for Major Departments Since July: Clinics: 29,466 people; day and night schools: 26,059 people; social education: 78,174 people; mutual aid cases: 1,507 people; dormitories (starting in February): 23,907 people; bathhouses: 74,070 people; reading rooms: 79,218 people; teahouses: 152,559 people; recreation rooms: 67,608 people; canteens (starting in April): 3,702 people; mobile medical services: 1,530 people.

Establishment of the City Zoo Pigeon Research Association - Shen Xiangrui Reports on the Preparatory Process - Articles of Association Amended and Approved by the Bureau of Education 138

The Shanghai Municipal Zoo has been preparing for the Pigeon Research Association for several months and has now been completed. Therefore, yesterday at 3:30 in the afternoon, the inaugural meeting was held at the Social Education Society near the Banfang on Penglai Road. The details are presented below.

Comrades Present

The pigeon raising comrades who arrived yesterday included Sun Xia, Tian Yi Mao Zhang Wuyan, Shen Baode, Xu Zhengyun, Gan Runhe, Zhou Yimin, Chen Zhaoyuan, Shen Xiangrui, Wang Qiangyuan, Li Xinming, Jiang Xiangfan, Xia Yongzhen, Kong Xiangyi, Chen Qiyun, and more than ten others. Shen Xiangrui was the chairman and Kong Xiangyi was the recorder.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony, the chairman first reported on the preparatory process and future prospects. His speech said that in view of the fact that using carrier pigeons to transmit messages can make up for the inadequacy of scientific communication, the city held the first Shanghai City Pigeon Race on May 9 of this year. It was approved by the Ministry of Military Affairs and the city's party and government agencies, and the participants were enthusiastic. However, the results of the competition were far less than the foreign records. It is deeply felt that it is difficult to compete with the carrier pigeons of the great powers if we do not rise up quickly to study. Therefore, on June 30, carrier pigeon comrades in the city were summoned to the park to solicit opinions and hold a preparatory meeting for the Pigeon Research Association. On July 5, membership forms were sent out, and a draft of the articles of association was prepared and submitted to the Bureau of Education for record. Later, on the 30th of last month, an order was issued to copy and distribute the amended articles of association of the association. Therefore, on August 1, letters were sent to all comrades to convene the inaugural meeting. Today, I am very pleased that all comrades have come despite 冒 (indistinct). In the future, I hope that the meeting will be attended on time, give great opinions, and work together to promote progress. The chair should 集 (collect) the strengths and do its best to promote it, in order to improve the breed and increase the flight speed, so as to keep pace with the carrier pigeons of various countries.

The Shanghai Sauce Garden Industry Association, for the sake of tax-free inferior soy sauce on the market, mixed and sold in various places, united with the industry associations of various cities and counties in the five provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei to petition, and after chemical examination by the Central Health Testing Institute, it was found to be toxic and harmful to health. The original text presented to Zhu Tingqi, director of the Salt Affairs Department, is recorded as follows. Presentation is for tax-free toxic and fake soy sauce, mixed and sold in various places, infringing on business, affecting national tax, and endangering people's livelihood.
