Shen Bao Medical Weekly

Medical Professionals' Assistance in the Anti-Smoking Campaign 194

— Song Guobin

Since Chairman Chiang took office as the Anti-Smoking Supervisor-General, the anti-smoking policies have indeed been implemented with vigor and speed. Consequently, the Shanghai Anti-Smoking Committee was established, and subsequently, anti-smoking branches were established in various provinces, cities, and counties. The prohibition of smoking, the prohibition of the grain tax levied on opium, the prohibition of trafficking, and the prohibition of transportation have yielded truly remarkable results. However, upon careful consideration, it is evident that medical professionals play a crucial role in assisting the anti-smoking campaign. The examination of smokers and the detoxification of opium addicts are almost entirely dependent on the involvement of medical professionals. Nevertheless, I believe that medical professionals can provide even greater assistance beyond examination and detoxification, namely, reporting to the authorities when opium addiction is discovered during patient diagnosis.

Some may argue: Doctors have a code of ethics that they must uphold, and preserving the privacy of patients is a key aspect of medical ethics. Anyone who discloses a patient's secrets without cause is subject to imprisonment under the law, and fellow professionals would be ashamed to associate with them. Doesn't your proposal risk violating criminal law and undermining medical ethics? I would respond: Matters vary in importance, and actions require adaptability. Judicious balance is the key. The anti-smoking campaign concerns the rise and fall of the nation, while maintaining confidentiality concerns the personal fortunes of an individual. Comparing the two in terms of importance, the former is greater, and the latter is smaller! Furthermore, I have heard that the new Italian criminal law stipulates that if doctors discover alcohol abuse during patient diagnosis, they must report it to the authorities; otherwise, they will be fined! This is because alcohol can disrupt social order. A patient's alcohol abuse is a patient's secret, yet Italian doctors do not allow the need for confidentiality to affect public safety. They truly understand what matters most. Does the impact of opium on the nation not outweigh the impact of alcohol on public safety by a hundred or a thousand times? I have also heard that doctors must report the discovery of infectious diseases to the authorities; otherwise, they will be fined! This is because the spread of epidemics can harm the public. A patient's illness is a patient's secret, yet doctors do not allow the need for confidentiality to affect public health. They truly understand how to balance priorities. Italy views the disruption of social order as no less significant than the spread of epidemics, hence the responsibility to report is entrusted to doctors. I would argue that the harm of opium is far greater than that of epidemics. Discovering opium addicts is like discovering patients with infectious diseases. Why should it be unacceptable? How does this conflict with medical confidentiality?

Humble Suggestions for the Ministry of Health to Urgently Establish Special Medical Training Classes 195

— Chen Aiyun

This article was previously submitted as a formal request to the Ministry of Health by yours truly. Now, in accordance with the Ministry's approval number 257, which stipulates that it should be retained for reference, I will publicly disclose the main points of the submission, hoping to draw the attention of fellow professionals to this matter. (Aiyun's Postscript)

I recall that during a meeting of the Central Political Council in 1930, Central Committee member Dai Jitao proposed expanding medical and health education. The proposal stated, "...Given the urgent need for medical personnel in our country, it is imperative to address the current problem of cultivating and supplying medical professionals. At the same time, we must gradually improve standards to realize a comprehensive and universal medical system that suits current conditions and avoids any neglect. The goal of this expansion is to achieve a ratio of one doctor per thousand people within thirty years... The development of medical and health knowledge and the popularization of talent are crucial for saving the nation from decline and are fundamental to people's livelihood... The current difficulties in people's lives mean that even middle-class families find it difficult to cultivate a medical student..." Mr. Dai, recognizing the lack of new medical personnel in our country, sought to utilize the government's power to achieve the popularization of scientific medicine domestically. Hence, this proposal was made. However, in reality, time has passed, the news has faded, and it remains nothing more than a pie in the sky, adding a few more strokes to the official files.

Looking at the current number of doctors registered with the Ministry of Health, there are only five or six thousand in the entire country. Distributing this small number of doctors among our country, which boasts a population of 400 million, is like using a cartload of firewood to put out a burning cart of firewood, a cup of water to extinguish a burning cartload of fuel. If we are to talk about popularizing modern medicine and achieving a ratio of one doctor per thousand people within thirty years, I truly wonder how many thirty-year periods it will take!

Our country is founded on agriculture, and farmers constitute the largest segment of the population. The health of farmers is fundamental to a strong nation. From this perspective, rural medical and health care are very important, and the need for rural doctors is naturally even more pressing. However, due to the small number of modern doctors, it is difficult to distribute them to rural areas. While this may not seem problematic in normal times, if an epidemic breaks out domestically, we will feel helpless and unable to provide relief. In summary, given the urgent need for doctors in our country and the difficulty of producing new doctors, why hasn't the authorities paid any attention to this important issue?

In a time when there is such a shortage of new medical personnel and such an urgent need for new medical personnel in rural areas, I believe there is still a way to remedy the situation through training. In the past, there was a temporary provision for granting certificates, but in reality, many doctors who met the criteria failed to register due to the expiration of the provision. These doctors may not have extensive theoretical knowledge but possess considerable experience. While they cannot compete with graduates of formal medical schools, they are certainly better than untrained practitioners who lack scientific knowledge. This group of people, who already possess a considerable amount of modern medical knowledge and skills and are around thirty years old, mostly live in rural areas and enjoy considerable trust. Now, because they are not registered, they are forced to cease practice. This not only creates problems for their livelihoods and the livelihoods of their families but also causes panic in rural areas that already feel the shortage of medical care. Furthermore, once these doctors become unemployed, it may be impossible for them to find alternative occupations at their age. Therefore, the government authorities should find a way to provide relief!

My idea is that if the Ministry of Health were to establish a "Special Medical Training Class," it could recruit these doctors for training, providing them with an opportunity for further education. This would not only supplement the insufficient number of doctors but also achieve a greater effect with less effort. These doctors could then be distributed to townships and villages, assisting the government in promoting rural health to save the nation from decline. On the other hand, this would also provide relief to these people, preventing them from becoming unemployed and helping them maintain their family's livelihood. This would bring significant benefits to the nation, the people's livelihood, and rural medical and health care. This method can be said to be superior to the provision for granting certificates. Therefore, the urgent establishment of a Special Medical Training Class by the Ministry of Health is a crucial task for addressing the current national health situation, alleviating the shortage of new medical personnel, and promoting rural medical and health care.

Regarding the implementation, it would be best if the Ministry of Interior's Department of Health and the National Economic Council's Health Division jointly organized it. They could start by piloting the first Special Medical Training Class in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. The qualifications for admission should be limited to those who met the criteria for the provision for granting certificates but failed to register due to its expiration, and who can provide proof from the local government's Public Security Bureau from 1930 to 1933, proving that they possess the ability of a doctor. Those who meet these criteria should be admitted without examination. The training should last for one year, and those who pass the examination upon completion should be granted a supplementary medical certificate, allowing them to practice medicine. Given the current national financial difficulties, it seems appropriate to charge tuition, lecture fees, practical fees, and boarding fees to cover the operating expenses of the class. Since the training only lasts for one year, the financial burden for each person would be at most around two hundred and fifty yuan, which each student should be able to afford. As for the faculty, senior personnel from the Ministry of Health, the Economic Council's Health Division, and the Central Three Offices could be hired to take on the role. In this way, I believe the Ministry of Health could pilot the first class. Regarding this plan, the senior doctors Song Guosheng and Pang Jingzhou have mentioned it in medical commentaries, and Doctor Xia Canglin has also published on it in the Medical Affairs Journal. The results in the future will surely be considerable.

Recent Tuberculosis Prevention Efforts in Italy 196

— Ding Huikang

Italy, governed by Fascism, has recently adopted a purely Fascist approach to tuberculosis prevention. All tuberculosis prevention agencies and facilities are completely under the control of the central government. The following anti-tuberculosis decree has been implemented: hospitals or clinics are not permitted to admit or examine any tuberculosis patients without the central government having received a formal report from the patient's family. Furthermore, mothers with tuberculosis are not allowed to recuperate at home; otherwise, their children must be immediately removed to another location for isolation. Within one week of formal reporting, patients must be admitted to a sanatorium for treatment, and their homes must be disinfected. All hospitals have uniform regulations and standards for implementing tuberculosis prevention and treatment. For example, Milan province, covering an area of 2,801 cubic kilometers, has a population of two million. It has 23 tuberculosis guidance centers, six sanatoriums with a total of 2,500 beds, and 17 tuberculosis hospitals with a total of 2,925 beds. In addition, there are tuberculosis hospitals affiliated with public health insurance agencies, with 3,000 beds, and three tuberculosis prevention sanatoriums with a total of 1,000 beds. All tuberculosis guidance centers are equipped with X-ray, artificial pneumothorax, and bacterial testing equipment. They also have comprehensive disinfection equipment and sputum disinfection facilities, and most are connected to major hospitals. Private practitioners generally cooperate with expert physicians from the various tuberculosis guidance centers.

The economic resources for tuberculosis prevention come from a five-lire surcharge on all transportation tickets throughout Italy each week. In addition, several museums have increased their admission fees by ten lire on certain dates. In Milan province, each resident must pay one lira per year for tuberculosis prevention (equivalent to two dimes in Chinese currency). In 1931, Milan province held a tuberculosis flower sale, raising a total of 3.46 million lire. In recent years, its tuberculosis prevention efforts have been very successful, and the mortality rate from tuberculosis has gradually decreased. In 1930, 2,613 people died from tuberculosis in Milan province, while in 1932, the number was 2,343.

Given the social conditions in our country, there is no doubt that tuberculosis prevention is even more important than in any other country. Last year, Mayor Wu, Li Tingan, Yan Fuqing, my father, and others initiated the China Tuberculosis Association, which is a pressing need for our time. However, the financial income relies on the collection of membership fees. I believe that instead of recruiting a small number of members, mostly based on the face of introducers, even if they join this year, it will not be possible to force them to rejoin next year. Even if someone joins, it will take up a certain amount of time and energy from all parties each year. It would be better to learn from Italy's past wisdom and broadly levy tuberculosis prevention funds. The cost to each person is minimal, and since it concerns public welfare, the public will naturally be happy to assist. By accumulating small amounts, we can achieve greater results with less effort. With sufficient funding, our country's tuberculosis prevention efforts will surely increase in effectiveness, and in a few years, it will not be difficult to catch up with other countries. I submit this to the members of the association for their consideration. (Sent from the Pulmonary Research Institute, University of Hamburg, Germany)

Constipation and Laxatives 197

— Yue Qi

—Medical Stories, No. 6—

American medical doctor Logan Clendening, in his famous book "The Human Body," has a passage on "constipation" that is quite insightful. I quote it here:

Some patients say: "I have been suffering from constipation for nearly ten years." Some say: "My depression and continuous fatigue are all due to constipation." Several years ago, a London doctor wrote an article stating

Page 16

that constipation can cause neurasthenia, stomach ulcers, chest tumors, and even tuberculosis. He said that everyone should have their colon removed. But he did not have his own colon removed because he said his colon was very good. Most doctors believe that constipation is the root of all diseases.

Based on my personal experience, I find this unreliable. Most of the patients who come to me for constipation do not actually have symptoms of constipation. Let me give an example. One day, a patient came and said that he was suffering from constipation. Although he took laxatives every day, they were ineffective and asked me to find a way to treat him. To test whether the patient was truly suffering from constipation, I asked him to eat a piece of opaque food so that I could use X-rays to observe the digestive process. This was on Monday at ten in the morning. At four in the afternoon, the patient came again. The examination showed that the food had left the stomach and entered the intestines. I instructed the patient to stop taking laxatives that night in order to calculate the natural rate of food digestion and asked him to come again at noon the next day. This time, the food had moved into the transverse colon. I instructed him again to not take laxatives that night and to come again on the third day. This time, the food was no longer in the intestines. So I asked him: "Did you have a bowel movement this morning?" He replied with a surprised expression: "Yes, it's strange, this is the first time in years that I've had such a natural bowel movement." For years, this patient had been taking laxatives every day, never thinking that a bowel movement without laxatives would be even smoother. This is because laxatives constantly irritate the inner wall of the intestines, and the resulting feeling of fullness makes him feel that his intestinal tract is never empty.

In this way, taking laxatives actually causes constipation.

After reading this passage, we can understand that diagnosing whether constipation is real or not is an important task for doctors. Related to this is the fact that laxatives should not be taken lightly.

Many laxatives were discovered by chance. A laxative called Epsom Salts (chemical composition is magnesium sulfate) was discovered in 1618 in a spring called Epsom on Dons Hill. According to legend, a farmer named Henry Wicks drove a herd of cattle to the spring on Dons Hill to drink water. Strangely, the cattle took one sip of the water and refused to drink any more. He tasted it himself and found that it was salty and bitter. Of course, he told his neighbors about this strange discovery. The local people began to use this spring water as an external application for treating skin ulcers and soreness, and it proved to be effective. A nobleman named Dudley North first tried using it as an internal medicine and found that it had a laxative effect. He then wrote an article publishing his discovery. As a result, Epsom Salts became a common laxative at the time.

Phenolphthalein is a new laxative. The history of this laxative's discovery is quite interesting. Before becoming a laxative, it was a common material in chemical laboratories because it has a property of turning red when it encounters alkali and remaining colorless when it encounters acid. Several years ago, the Hungarian government enacted a law stipulating that white wine must be mixed with a certain amount of phenolphthalein in order to test whether the wine was adulterated with inferior goods. After this law was implemented, dysentery spread rampantly throughout Hungary, indicating that the previously considered harmless phenolphthalein had strong laxative properties. At the same time, magicians who performed the "turning water into wine" trick often suffered from diarrhea after performing the trick. It turned out that the clear water in the pot contained sodium carbonate, and the empty glass cup that received the clear water poured from the pot had been pre-filled with a few drops of phenolphthalein. The alkaline water, when it came into contact with the phenolphthalein, naturally turned wine-red. Each time the fake wine was made, the performer himself took a sip, deliberately pretending to taste the wine in order to dazzle the audience. This is how he ingested several doses of laxative in a row, and diarrhea was naturally the inevitable result. Phenolphthalein can be mixed into candy and gum, so it is a laxative that is easy for children to take.

According to Doctor Clendening, the most natural laxative is not any medicine but vegetables. Because the cellulose contained in vegetables is not digested but remains in the intestines to promote intestinal excretion. This is the only type of laxative that is truly beneficial and harmless.

Popular Lectures on Modern Venereology (12) 198

— Chen Shengbai (Compiled) Yin Muqiang (Proofread)

Part Two Gonorrhea

D. If gonorrhea persists for a long time and the virus spreads, then, based on anatomical and physiological relationships, the following may occur:

(1) Paraurethritis: A small amount of pus is discharged from the paraurethral ducts. A slightly hard, rope-like object or nodule can be felt locally.

(2) Periurethral infiltration: Forms a hard cord. Abscesses may also form, requiring incision.

(3) Cowper's gland inflammation: Painful nodules occur between the scrotum and the anus, especially painful during bowel movements. In severe cases, the inflammation spreads to the surrounding tissues, causing cellulitis.

(4) Prostatitis: In the rectum, swelling, hardening, and pain of the prostate gland can be palpated. There is also a subjective sensation of pain in the prostate region, frequent urination, stabbing pain during ejaculation, or seminal leakage. In more severe cases, inflammation occurs in most or all of the prostate, accompanied by chills, shivering, fever, and marked frequent urination, pain in the perineum or rectal region during defecation and sitting, and if it turns into an abscess, it often ruptures into the urethra, temporarily discharging a large amount of pus and relieving the symptoms. It may also rupture into the rectum, causing rectal gonorrhea, or rupture into the bladder or perineum or pelvic connective tissue, or become thrombophlebitis, sepsis, and other systemic diseases, but this is extremely rare.

(5) Seminal vesiculitis: Particularly painful during ejaculation. The semen appears bloody and purulent.

(6) Epididymitis: Often accompanied by chills, shivering, and fever. The epididymis is swollen and painful. At this time, it often impairs sperm production, leading to infertility.

(7) Cystitis: Severe pain, urgency to urinate, frequent urination, discomfort, heaviness, and pain in the lower abdomen. Sometimes, the internal sphincter spasms and causes urinary incontinence.

(8) Ureteritis and pyelonephritis

At this time, there are chills, shivering, high fever, headache, vomiting, and pain in the lower back.

(9) Others, such as balanitis, phimosis, and urethral stricture. All organs related to the male urinary and reproductive system may be susceptible to disease.

(II) Gonorrhea in Women The symptoms of gonorrhea in women differ due to anatomical differences. The differing symptoms are described below:

A. Skene's gland inflammation Local redness and swelling. A small amount of pus leaks out when compressed.

B. Bartholin's gland inflammation This gland is frequently affected. The symptoms are a fluctuating tumor bulging within the labia minora. The labia are red and swollen with severe pain. If it ruptures naturally, it will discharge a large amount of yellow-green pus.

C. Rectal gonorrhea Anatomically, a woman's vaginal wall is closely attached to the rectum, so rectal gonorrhea is common in women. Burning pain is felt, especially during bowel movements. Sometimes pus leaks out of the rectum. The skin around the anus is also red, swollen, and injured or ulcerated due to irritation from the secretions.

D. Others, such as vulvitis and vaginitis. Although the names are different, the symptoms are not particularly different from those of balanitis, phimosis, and urethritis in men. I will not elaborate further.

(III) Metastatic Gonorrhea Due to metastasis via blood or lymph circulation. Gonococcal arthritis, tenosynovitis, bursitis, endocarditis, etc., can occur. Each has its own specific symptoms, which are omitted here.

Common Sense on Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Health 199

— Tang Renjin

(58) Laryngeal Tuberculosis (Continued)

An inevitable symptom of this disease is hoarseness. In severe cases, the voice can be completely lost. There is also frequent coughing. If ulcers develop, there will be mucus-like purulent sputum. Patients feel some pain when swallowing. If infiltration or disintegration occurs at the entrance of the larynx, severe difficulty in swallowing will occur. Sometimes, aspiration may occur. When the patient coughs or speaks, they often feel pain in the throat. Breathing difficulty is usually absent unless there is significant inflammatory edema. In addition, patients often complain of fever. If we press on the larynx from the outside, the patient often feels pain. Sometimes, swelling can be palpated. This is because of secondary perichondritis. The changes in the pharynx are that the mucous membrane appears distinctly anemic and pale. This is also a unique symptom of this disease. The changes within the larynx are that the mucous membrane develops tuberculous infiltration and tuberculous ulcers. Therefore, in general, in patients with pulmonary tuberculosis, if their condition progresses, the infiltrated tissue caused by laryngeal tuberculosis will lose its resistance and disintegrate, forming a flat ulcer. The larger ones can sometimes reach the size of a pea. At this time, most patients suffer from difficulty in swallowing. In addition, it is important to note that in many patients, small, yellow, millet-sized nodules develop in the larynx due to blood circulation. These nodules soon rupture and form creeping superficial ulcers. At this point, if sputum is examined, tubercle bacilli are often present. Early diagnosis and early treatment are crucial for this disease. However, early diagnosis is not easy. This is because its symptoms, such as hoarseness, difficulty in swallowing, and suffocation, are also common in other laryngeal diseases. Moreover, laryngeal tuberculosis is often combined with acute or chronic catarrhal symptoms. Do not mistakenly regard these symptoms as catarrhal symptoms of pulmonary tuberculosis. Furthermore, it is especially important to distinguish it from other diseases such as syphilis, tumors, and hoarseness caused by nervous disorders. The most reliable diagnosis is examination with a laryngoscope. Therefore, patients with pulmonary tuberculosis should regularly undergo laryngoscopic examination by a specialist to check for local lesions. Do not miss the opportunity for early diagnosis and early treatment. This is of utmost importance.

The treatment methods for laryngeal tuberculosis are very complex and cannot be generalized. Because this disease is often a complication of pulmonary tuberculosis, general health care and treatment methods for pulmonary tuberculosis should be implemented first. Take in large amounts of nutritious food and pay attention to air regulation. As for local treatment of the disease, it can be divided into three types: drug therapy, surgical therapy, and light therapy. Drug therapy includes drug injection, drug application, drug corrosion, drug powder insufflation, and drug inhalation. Surgical therapy includes forceps removal, electrocautery, and tracheotomy. Among light therapies, artificial sun lamps with a device for directly irradiating the larynx and the lamp invented by the Austrian Viennese physician Mr. Huishilai are more effective. It is worth trying.

Medical Knowledge for Pain Relief (2) (6) 200

— Li Xing

Throat Pain

Tonsillitis and Pharyngitis: Tonsils, located on both sides of the throat, often become inflamed, causing pain with each inflammation. When inflamed, the tonsils become red and swollen, often with white spots. The body temperature can rise to 101 degrees Fahrenheit. The entire throat also becomes inflamed alongside the tonsillitis. Tonsillitis is caused by common throat bacteria becoming active during a cold. Inflammation usually subsides and returns to normal after several days. For tonsillitis treatment, severe cases require bed rest, while mild cases do not. A liquid diet is recommended. In addition, gargle with a throat medicine such as a mixture of one-quarter Hydrogen Peroxide (one-quarter Hydrogen Peroxide mixed with three-quarters water) or a 2% sodium borate solution, several times a day. Tonsils that become inflamed throughout the year should be removed to prevent bacteria from entering the heart and causing carditis, or entering the joints and causing rheumatism or arthritis.

Peritonsillar Abscess: Around the tonsils near the throat opening, bacteria often invade from the tonsils, causing inflammation and forming an abscess. Patients feel swelling and pain on one side of the throat and have difficulty swallowing. Upon opening the mouth, the tonsils and surrounding area are red and swollen. Patients also often experience chills and fever within one to two days. Before an abscess forms, treatment includes resting and applying hot and cold compresses to the neck. Once an abscess forms, it must be surgically incised to drain the pus.

Diphtheria or Throat Scarlatina: Most people now know that diphtheria is a very dangerous disease. Although people fear diphtheria, sometimes they are unaware when the disease strikes. Diphtheria often occurs imperceptibly, with the first sensation being a sore throat. Examination of the throat reveals a grayish-white membrane, and diphtheria bacteria can be found under a microscope or after culturing. Patients develop a fever of approximately 100 to 103 degrees Fahrenheit. Note that diphtheria is transmitted through close contact with infected individuals. The first priority upon contracting diphtheria is to inject diphtheria antitoxin serum as early as possible. Before the invention of antitoxin serum, an average of one in three diphtheria patients died. Since the use of diphtheria antitoxin serum, the mortality rate has significantly decreased, with approximately one in ten or twenty patients dying on average. It is also crucial to note that early injection of antitoxin serum results in a lower mortality rate, while late injection results in a higher mortality rate. According to statistics, the mortality rate for diphtheria patients injected with diphtheria antitoxin serum on the first day of illness is 15 per 1,000. The mortality rate for those injected on the second day is 34 per 1,000. The mortality rate for those injected on the third day is 69 per 1,000. The mortality rate for those injected on the fourth day is 109 per 1,000. The mortality rate for those injected on the fifth day is 150 per 1,000. The mortality rate for those not injected is 350 per 1,000. Let's compare: the mortality rate for those not injected is 25 times higher than for those injected on the first day. The mortality rate for those injected on the fifth day is ten times higher than for those injected on the first day. The mortality rate for those injected on the fourth day is approximately seven times higher than for those injected on the first day. The mortality rate for those injected on the third day is four and a half times higher than for those injected on the first day. The mortality rate for those injected on the second day is more than twice as high as for those injected on the first day. Diphtheria does not kill patients through throat pain, but through diphtheria toxin entering the blood, damaging the heart, or blocking the respiratory tract and suffocating the patient. In summary, the primary treatment for diphtheria throat pain is to inject diphtheria antitoxin serum, preferably on the first day of illness. Never treat it as a common sore throat.

A Brief Discussion on Pulmonary Tuberculosis (6) (2) 201

— Hu Jiayan

Section 6: Renal Tuberculosis

In addition to detailed urine examination, there are two other examination procedures that are absolutely essential for accurately diagnosing this condition. The first is cystoscopy, which immediately reveals the condition of the mucous membrane. (Bladder tuberculosis is mostly caused by the downward spread of kidney tuberculosis; therefore, finding tuberculous lesions in the bladder can indirectly prove kidney tuberculosis.) Regarding whether the ureter is passable, and whether the kidney tuberculosis affects the right or left kidney, or both kidneys are affected, these important questions can be confirmed or denied by performing ureteral catheterization. The second is X-ray examination, which is crucial for demonstrating the shape and size of the kidney, as well as calcified lesions. Both of these examination methods should be performed by a specialist physician; otherwise, it will be difficult to distinguish between right and wrong, almost tantamount to calling a deer a horse!

Regarding the treatment of this disease, surgery may not be necessary in the early stages. The approach is generally similar to that of ordinary tuberculosis (chronic form) and chronic nephritis. Injections of tuberculin are sometimes very effective. Metal-based treatments are very likely to irritate the kidneys and should be avoided. X-ray therapy is also ineffective. If the disease is progressing or spreading, we should check the condition of the other kidney. If it is completely healthy, the diseased kidney can be surgically removed; this approach sometimes yields very good results. As for the patient's diet and daily life, they are the same as for ordinary pulmonary tuberculosis.

Page 17

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Mutual Assistance of the Oppressed 202

— Xing An

Calcutta, 26th: Gandhi today requested 350 million Indians to donate to the Red Cross to provide relief in Abyssinia, stating, "Mussolini's threat to all people of color around the world makes it impossible for India to remain indifferent. Although India is not a belligerent nation, as a member of the League of Nations, it should assist another member nation."

The conflict between Italy and Abyssinia is no longer merely a dispute between nations, but has involved the issue of race. Gandhi's call for people of color expresses his outrage. It is heard that Indians are expressing strong sympathy for Abyssinia. This situation will directly affect British colonial and East African policies.

Racial concepts, in a world where human interaction is becoming increasingly close, still exist in the minds of various races. The 20th-century world is evidently the world of white people. Therefore, people have developed the so-called fear of racial war. Many people predict that future wars will evolve from national disputes into racial conflicts.

In fact, this is perhaps an overestimation of future problems. Whether racial wars will occur in the future cannot, of course, be predicted. But at present, the phenomenon of people of the same race trampling on each other can still be seen everywhere. As long as there are conflicting interests, even people of the same race helping people of a different race is not considered strange. This is not only true of people of color, who each plot for their own benefit, but also of white people, who are known for their strong solidarity. Therefore, I believe that racial war, assuming it can occur, is far from today.

What is inevitable in the future is the struggle between the oppressed and the oppressors. The world today can be roughly divided into two major classes: the oppressed and the oppressors. The oppressed are generally weak nations, and the oppressors are the so-called great powers. The latter take sacrificing the interests of the former as a means of self-preservation. The former can only eke out an existence under the control and domination of the latter. The opposition between these two classes is irreconcilable. Once it breaks down in the future, a major struggle will immediately occur. This is a glorious war of the oppressed against the powerful. India's expression of sympathy for Abyssinia is, rather than being based on racial concepts, more accurately described as a form of mutual assistance among weak nations.

Racial war is formed from narrow racial concepts. The struggle between the oppressed and the oppressors, this meaning is great. Because true human equality can only be realized after the oppressed are liberated. Sun Yat-sen said that China's demand for freedom and equality requires uniting the world's weak nations and fighting together. This understanding is very clear. China's future outlet may lie here.

Green Lamp and Dream 203

— Xia Yin

(1) Green Lamp

Every night, wiping clean the green lamp on the corner of the table, a perplexed sentiment gently emerges from the bottom of my heart. This lonely wandering life has worn down my young life into a green lamp, containing the raging flames: gradually drifting away from those bright and joyful days.

This green lamp has accompanied me through so many difficult days! Under its green, serene light, I have never been idle in cultivating the necessities of life, and the beautiful dreams that many young people have. Lengthy and arduous labor has worn away my innocence. For the world, for life, a blurred black shadow unfolds, blocking the forbidden land of happiness that I long for. Making me acutely aware of the vagueness of the future and the cruelty of reality. Although all these only stir up my indignation, turning my fiery eyes to confront all the vile phenomena: not kneeling and kowtowing to life; not letting this bright red heart be tainted by the slightest flaw, as proud as a plum blossom in the snowy mountains, scattering its solitary fragrance in the icy wilderness

Page 18

of the vast wilderness.

Yes, I accept all the suffering cast upon me by the world, using my own strength to cultivate life, to obtain life. Not envying the happiness of others, but blessing my own efforts and struggles. Others will naturally inevitably see me as an unenterprising coward, a mediocre and worthless fool. But, I have my own views, ideals. These shallow and snobbish ridicule cannot shake my conviction. For myself, I am very clear that in this ordinary life, even the smallest bubbles and ripples contain many moving and admirable struggles, that is the sublimation of my blood, the sublimation of my sweat, the sublimation of my whole personality. For myself, it is all worthy of pride.

This is not an exaggerated and self-consoling argument. People are not like witless oxen, the purpose of endurance and cultivation is not in a short period of rest. They have a greater ideal, they want to cultivate a full field of green seedlings and hunger-saving rice in the dry and barren land.

Although, life is ultimately bitter. I will not forget the suffering of these days, gradually drifting away from those bright and joyful days, my young life has been worn down into a green lamp, containing the raging flames, letting passion hide in my heart. Naturally, for these difficult days, the gradually changing life, it is inevitable that it will stir up a sense of sadness at the bottom of my heart.

But, difficult days bring a difficult life. Life is originally climbing towards the road stretching out under one's feet. Even if this road is rugged and dangerous, one must clench one's teeth and crawl up!

Let those bright and joyful days drift away forever. Always be accompanied by the green lamp, use your own strength to cultivate life, to obtain life!

(2) Dream

Accompanying me through these long, lonely wandering days is the dream that is never finished. These dreams are so ordinary, always the same tune, dreaming that the universe is full of crimson and green flowers.

After seeing everything clearly, I often ask myself with determination.

—For the sake of cherishing my own youth, can't I end this illusory dream?

Naturally, as the days go by, I gradually feel the sadness in my heart, like a soft and greasy spider silk weaving and binding in my heart for no reason, even with the strength to shatter cauldrons and uproot mountains, I cannot tear away this delicate thing. So, I cannot help but gently sigh, I regret that my vitality also has weak factors. However——

—The war song of the mountain eagle is loud and clear, when the wind and rain come, it always cannot forget the peaceful mountains and forests.

Even the brave warriors on the battlefield have their "battlefield dreams", although I am stubborn, how can I escape this instinct?

Life is originally a stage for struggle. There will never be a time when the universe is full of crimson and green flowers!

For myself, I must take good care of myself, but also not forget that human vitality also has weak factors.

Summer Evening (Part 2) 204

— Ya Fei

At this time, the houses are all empty, all the people, big and small, male and female, have all escaped to the open space in front of the door: telling stories, making jokes, and some people are reporting some unreliable news heard from teahouses or the streets and alleys. Uncle Jinbao, however, is sitting alone on a white wooden stool, picking salt-fried beans and sipping white liquor, his wife is sitting on the bluestone beside him, feeding the child porridge.

There are also many older children who have each taken a glass bottle or duck eggshell to catch fireflies in the lawn.

"Be careful of snakes, insects, and centipedes; catching fireflies that will snatch your souls, catch them and use them for food!" The women are scolding their children like this, but those naughty children are unwilling to listen, if they don't catch them here, they run to the trellis of trichosanthes kirilowii to catch them again.

"Little... Dong people... got into... trouble..." A Jin, who is particularly fond of inquiring about gossip, has just returned from town drunk, humming an out-of-tune "Three Mothers Teach Son" in his mouth.

"You're happy! The rice for tomorrow's breakfast is still flying in the sky, but you still want to worship Huang Tang, worship urine!" His wife, leaning against a Toona sinensis tree, glared at him and said resentfully.

"Haha! Tomorrow, screw him, we'll figure it out after today!" He said, sitting down on the threshold; "Do you know? Today the Yin Gou family caught a thief stealing pumpkins."

"I guessed long ago that Bao Datian would go to town to inquire, there would always be news brought back." Sister-in-law Cai Bao said playfully.

"Alas! This world, everyone is about to starve to death, things are not growing firmly at all, there are so many thieves, stealing every day, who has such constant eyes to watch!" Father Si, who had not spoken for a long time, finally began to feel emotional.

The cool breeze of the summer evening blows gently towards this open space, driving away all the heat of the day; so everyone feels a little tired, and everyone is looking towards their own house.

Fragments of Summer 205

— Mo Jia

Thinking of my home in the south

Oh, the May weather of my beloved hometown! At the end of the mountains, at the far end of the sea, the mild climate of the south, there is a clear sky, a beautiful scenery, although summer is coming to an end, but there, it is the season for late-ripening longans, the season for late-blooming oranges to give off fragrance, and the season for late-ripening red grape bunches to come on the market. These fruits, which carry sweet or perhaps sour flavors, are the only gifts that accompany you to eliminate the long summer. When noon arrives, the house is a bit stuffy, so bring a branch, or a bunch of longans, along with a bamboo mat, spread it under the shade of several banyan trees in front of the house, slowly peeling the longan shells, the lychee shells, eating them, eating them, you probably don't need a fan, the wind has already blown in gusts from the fields, blowing up the fragrance of oranges. And thinking of longans, one thinks of a section of gentle feelings that contain honey juice like longans, at that time, there was a young woman living in the neighborhood, her family planted a clump of old longans, which always bloomed the latest and bore fruit the latest, waiting until they were rotten ripe, when the longan festival was over, hers could just be picked, the size was particularly large, and it was also particularly flavorful, and this young woman, her own name was exactly Longan, because she had a pair of shiny, round eyeballs like longan pits, and a skin color as black as the color of longans, and she had been particularly fond of longans since she was a child, her name, Longan Sister, was what people had gotten used to calling her. Whenever her family picked longans, she would always bring a few handfuls to my house herself. Longan Sister, Longan Sister, the weather is so hot, you still come out yourself, keep it for yourself, we have already eaten a lot. I said with an almost joking tone, she stood there a little shyly, smiling lightly, her longan-like beads shining with charming black luster, you always like to tease, saying she pursed her lips, threw a handful of longans in my direction, and left. Looking at her pretty back, my heart couldn't help but move, I did praise her simple smile, her pure words, but I couldn't lightly tell anyone the secrets in my heart, these secrets I could only let it quietly hide deep in my heart, in the first year after I left home, Longan Sister had already, at the suggestion of her parents, married a stranger, my unknown thoughts also became an unknown eternal regret. Three years ago, I once went back, coincidentally Longan Sister also came back to her parents' home during my return, but she was already holding a child, it was still summer, I saw her sitting in front of her own house, it was evening, she bared her chest to feed the child milk, Longan Sister, so fast, do you still recognize me? She looked at me with a little shyness and smiled, I thought of the unmarried Longan Sister when I was young, I stirred up my unknown and forgotten thoughts, I secretly felt sadness for a person losing her youth for no reason. Now that I have left my hometown again for several years, Longan Sister should have raised several children again.

2. Midnight

At night, the house is still hot and stuffy, without a bit of wind, there is wind outside, but because the window lattice is small, and it faces north, it can't blow in, people sit still, and sweat flows non-stop, so I had to turn off the light, thinking of eliminating a little of the heat of the light, but as soon as the light was turned off, the mosquitoes became proud, buzzing and making a big fuss, looking for an opportunity to bite hard on the body, after driving away this one, that one was biting on the back again. There was no way, I had to sneak out, just walking out the door, a cool breeze blew towards my face, my feeling suddenly relaxed, I took a light breath, outside it was really like another world, the house seemed like a steamer compared to it, so terrible. Walking along the pebble path. The surroundings were quiet, the night was deep, there was a large moon in the sky, the silvery light melted the earth in the sway of mercury, the stars were very sparse, I casually sat on a lawn, looking at the misty sky, a light and crisp mood, my heart was also light and loose because of this, but when that occasional lonely wild goose call flew past in mid-air, although it flew far away, the desolate feeling stayed unshakably in my heart, and I was always too concerned about the moon in the sky, the twinkling stars, especially fond of that light and cool wind, often sitting in a daze in this empty and melting midnight heart, sometimes even when the moon sinks and the stars bathe, I am still unwilling to leave, and I am always given a little illness by midnight because of this.

People 206

— Cun Yin

Do not let kindness and sincerity leave you;

Bind them around your neck,

Write them on the tablet of your heart.

——Prelude

Interlude:

I will go to the mountain of myrrh,

I will go to the hill of frankincense.

Until the day breathes and the shadows flee,

I will return.

——Song of Songs 4:6.

Quietly, a pink cloud floats over the top of the house.

In that clean white building, the nurses are saying, "Oh, it's night again."

They are wearing white clothes and white hats. Their faces, skin, and hair are not white. They are very quiet and demure, like a flock of little birds nesting in their nests.

"Oh, it's night again."

"Yes. Dr. Ling said that in half an hour, if the woman in room three still hasn't given birth, they will have to operate on her."

"Hmm. Amen."

"Amen." Making the sign of the cross. The two of them separated.

Gently pushing open the white door of room three.

A desolate, painful scream clearly echoed in the room.

"Nurse, it hurts, save me..." The pregnant woman's face was very pale, as if someone had stabbed her leg with a small knife. She tossed and turned on the bed.

"Nurse, please save her." An elderly woman accompanying the pregnant woman said so sorrowfully, wiping away her tears.

"Don't let her roll around on the bed! The doctor will be here soon." She arranged the white cotton, gauze, and the shiny white tray, shiny pliers, and rubber gloves. Then, she pushed open the door and walked out.

And the pregnant woman's painful scream was incessantly pouring out like smoke from a chimney.

"Help!"

One of the nurses said, "Lord, save her!"

Dr. Ling pushed open the door of room three. Seven or eight young nurses followed him quietly and demurely.

The pregnant woman's face was almost as white as the white coat worn by the doctors.

"Doctor, please save her." The elderly woman said timidly.

"Hmm." Dr. Ling nodded. He stood in front of the bed and observed the pregnant woman's movements. Then, he pressed the pregnant woman's pulse.

"Oh, it hurts, it hurts, doctor, save me!" The

Page 19

Page 20

Page 21

pregnant woman, whose lips had also turned gray, suddenly screamed wildly again.

After looking at the pregnant woman, Dr. Ling turned his head and said to the young nurses:

"It's a difficult birth. Let's pray for her.

So everyone knelt down in an orderly manner. Even the elderly woman who was chanting "Amitabha" was told to kneel down.

Then one of the young nurses recited a prayer.

The pregnant woman's pain intensified. The air was filled with solemnity.

"Amen." Everyone made the sign of the cross.

The prayer was over. And the pregnant woman's painful scream had become low and hoarse.

When it dawned, the nurses performed a second prayer for the pregnant woman, in the surgical room.

Before long, one of the nurses walked out of the door and said to the elderly woman who was sitting on the long bench outside the surgical room door, chanting "Amitabha":

"Your daughter-in-law has died of suffocation. Because the surgery was performed too late."

"Then the child, is the boy alright?" the elderly woman asked quickly.

"He is very well, madam."

"Hmm, that's lucky! Amitabha!" The elderly woman's anxiety seemed to lessen. She suddenly fixed her gaze on the nurse and asked:

"Hey, nurse, where are the clothes my daughter-in-law changed out of?"

"They were probably left in the sickroom. Is something the matter?"

"Hmm, were you the one who changed her clothes?" Her expression softened.

"Yes."

"Then please tell me, does she have the small leather wallet with the money in her pocket?" Her tears had also dried up.

"I don't know about that. What are you planning to do, madam?"

"I plan to buy some eggs to dye red eggs."

"Madam, can you still dye red eggs when someone has died?"

"Huh, it's a woman who died! It doesn't count for much. Why can't I dye red eggs? Amitabha." The elderly woman opened her mouth and smiled, continuing, "Nurse, can you lead me to see the baby boy? Oh, maybe she also has a purse in her pocket. Let me take the purse first and then go see the baby boy."

Narrative Song 207

Tang Zhuping - Falling Golden Fan

Huaguang (1480) 3:00 PM to 3:45 PM

Opening: "Fisherman's Footprints"

Skilled in navigating ships, he roams everywhere. The "Myriad Homes of Spring" sails heavily on rivers. His body is accustomed to being at home anywhere in the world. He has no worries about food and clothing, living a carefree life. Why bother distinguishing between noble and lowly by attire? One's fate is entirely determined by their inherent character. The copper coins he earns are spent as quickly as they come. In his leisure, he enjoys drinking alone. By himself at the top of the building, he toasts to Li Bai [a famous poet], nodding, clapping, and laughing heartily. Who knew the tavern owner had a preference for beauty? He secretly teases the fisherman's daughter, Xiao Yu. Luckily, the gentleman sees this with a cold eye. He wants to call the local constable and neighbors. Who is without sin for raping a woman? He doesn't care about making amends early. He reluctantly writes a confession in his own hand. Every year, he drinks and racks up a tab. The word "tab" is better off nonexistent. In this life and the next, he will have no bar tab. Who dares to treat me coldly in the future? He secretly helps to save the beautiful maiden by assassinating the traitor Liang Ji. Truly, he is a little man of the world.

News 212

The "Red Light Arts Society" is an organization of high village students from various schools in Shanghai. They have excellent results. It is said that Ms. Chen Meiying, director of the society's singing group, will lead a group of ladies to audition at major radio stations.

The Baijia Singing Society was founded in Shanghai by Nelson & Co. and members of the press, including Wang Yong, Huang Jianren, and Jin Zhijing. The society has been in preparation for a long time and has a large internal scale. It has now selected high-level male and female singers. It is rumored that they will soon broadcast special programs on major radio stations in the city. The society is now recruiting male and female members. Anyone with aspirations and a love of music can join. Send a simple letter of inquiry with a one-cent stamp attached. The mailing address is currently temporarily located at Mr. Huang Jianren, 2nd Floor, 205 Shandong Road, or Mr. Cheng Jun of Nelson & Co., 4th Floor, Jingyun Building, Beijing Road.

New News from the Performing Arts Experimental Institute 213

Since Mr. Lu Shi took over the Performing Arts Experimental Institute, he has been working hard to reorganize it. The new site that the institute is scheduled to move to is currently under repair. It is expected to be able to move in by the end of this month or the beginning of next month. Currently, it is temporarily using the old site for office work and classes. Many people have signed up for the institute's second round of student recruitment. Today (the 5th) is the first examination period, and the second examination period will be on the 12th.

Mr. Wang, Tang Jie, is shooting exterior scenes for "Mr. Wang Goes to the Countryside" in the Suzhou countryside. The news has spread far and wide, and more than 500 people come to watch every day.

Little A Yuan, Huang Naishuang, has a deep appreciation for elegance. In her spare time, she often catches shrimp and frogs by the river, which is quite poetic. Zuo Ming even gave her the elegant title of "woman poet."

Half the Sky This Week 215

The crew of the new film "Sea Burial" returned from Yantai yesterday.

The "Sea Burial" crew worked on the Shandong coast for nearly two months. Every day, intelligence personnel recorded the work in detail for public release.

Interior scenes for "Sea Burial" will be shot soon.

The ship used in "Sea Burial" has already been built.

It is said that the sound film "Two Brothers" was originally named "Liu Xiaofeng."

Lu Lixia told people that "Two Brothers" is the only one of her works that she is relatively satisfied with.

Special Feature on Situ Huimin, Director of "Goddess of Freedom" 216

Situ Huimin, the writer and director of Diantong's "Goddess of Freedom," used his "personal" experience of the "May Fourth" movement and the revolutionary Northern Expedition as the weft, and a struggling woman in a turbulent era as the warp to write this "Goddess of Freedom." He also boldly and carefully directs this film with his extensive experience in photography. The magnificent revolutionary historical facts in the play require him to have a firm and controlled hand to express. Seeing his style in every crowd scene is like seeing him in person: concise and experienced, without hesitation or doubt. But in places that require care, he also has a more humble attitude. In order to obtain historical materials about the "May Fourth" era in the play, he went to Hangzhou twice to conduct on-the-ground investigations into the social customs of Hangzhou at that time. In addition, with his past experience in set design and sound recording, "the overall success of the visuals and sound of 'Goddess of Freedom' can be predicted with certainty."
